<script>
// ============================================
// STATE
// ============================================
const state = {
    apiUrl: window.location.origin !== 'null' && !window.location.origin.startsWith('file') ? window.location.origin : 'http://localhost:3001',
    items: [], allItems: [], dumps: [], pumps: [], recipes: [],
    watchlist: new Set(), isConnected: false,
    currentSort: 'realistic', currentFilter: '', verdictFilter: 'all', lastUpdate: new Date(),
    mappingById: {}, prevPrices: {},
    cachedMapping: null, cachedLatest: null, cachedVolData: {},
    lastFullRefresh: 0, lastDumpCheck: 0,
    fullRefreshInterval: 45000, dumpCheckInterval: 8000,
    viewMode: 'table',
    dpHistory: [],      // { time, dumps, pumps } for chart
    sniperHistory: [],  // { time, severity, count } for sniper chart
    priceSnapshots: {},  // itemId -> [{ time, avg }] for sparklines
    priceHistory: {},    // itemId -> [{ time, price, vol }] rolling window
    charts: {},          // chart instances
    dumpLog: [],         // { time, itemId, name, percentChange, type } - max 100 entries
    webhookUrl: 'REDACTED_WEBHOOK_URL',
    autoAlertsEnabled: true,
    notificationsEnabled: false,
    showIntel: false,  // Market intel hidden by default, expandable per-item
    lastAlertTimes: {},  // itemId-type -> timestamp for rate limiting
    lastGlobalAlert: 0,  // global rate limit
    alertsThisHour: [], // timestamps of alerts sent this hour (max 6/hr)
    discordAlertedItems: {}, // itemId -> timestamp, prevents flicker re-alerts
    refreshCountdown: 0,
    priceBaselines: {},  // { normal1h, normal5m, lastSeen } per item
    fetchCache: {},      // { [endpoint]: { data, time } } for fetch deduplication
    lastRenderHash: '',  // for renderTopFlips optimization
    lastDumpsHash: '',   // for renderDumpsPumps optimization
};

// ============================================
// SETTINGS/DISCORD WEBHOOK
// ============================================
function loadSettings() {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('gfo_webhook_url');
    const autoAlerts = localStorage.getItem('gfo_auto_alerts');
    const watchlistSaved = localStorage.getItem('gfo_watchlist');
    const notifEnabled = localStorage.getItem('gfo_notifications_enabled');
    const showIntel = localStorage.getItem('gfo_showIntel');
    if (saved) state.webhookUrl = saved;
    // state.webhookUrl already has the default hardcoded, so it works out of the box
    if (autoAlerts !== null) state.autoAlertsEnabled = autoAlerts === 'true';
    if (notifEnabled !== null) state.notificationsEnabled = notifEnabled === 'true';
    if (showIntel !== null) state.showIntel = showIntel === 'true';
    if (watchlistSaved) {
        try {
            const ids = JSON.parse(watchlistSaved);
            state.watchlist = new Set(ids);
        } catch {}
    }
    document.getElementById('webhookInput').value = state.webhookUrl || '';
    if (state.autoAlertsEnabled) document.getElementById('autoAlertToggle').classList.add('on');
    const notifToggle = document.getElementById('notifToggle');
    if (notifToggle && state.notificationsEnabled) notifToggle.classList.add('on');
    const intelToggle = document.getElementById('showIntelToggle');
    if (intelToggle && state.showIntel) intelToggle.classList.add('on');
    // Request notification permission if Notification API is available
    if ('Notification' in window && Notification.permission === 'default') {
        // Will ask when user first visits Dump Sniper tab
    }
}

function saveSettings() {
    state.webhookUrl = document.getElementById('webhookInput').value.trim();
    localStorage.setItem('gfo_webhook_url', state.webhookUrl);
    localStorage.setItem('gfo_auto_alerts', state.autoAlertsEnabled);
    localStorage.setItem('gfo_notifications_enabled', state.notificationsEnabled);
    localStorage.setItem('gfo_showIntel', state.showIntel);
}

function loadWatchlist() {
    try {
        const saved = localStorage.getItem('gfo_watchlist');
        if (saved) { JSON.parse(saved).forEach(id => state.watchlist.add(id)); }
    } catch {}
}
function saveWatchlist() {
    localStorage.setItem('gfo_watchlist', JSON.stringify(Array.from(state.watchlist)));
}

function toggleSettingsModal() {
    const modal = document.getElementById('settingsModal');
    modal.classList.toggle('active');
    if (modal.classList.contains('active')) {
        document.getElementById('webhookInput').value = state.webhookUrl || '';
    }
}

function toggleAutoAlerts(toggle) {
    state.autoAlertsEnabled = !state.autoAlertsEnabled;
    toggle.classList.toggle('on');
    saveSettings();
}

async function testDiscordWebhook() {
    const url = document.getElementById('webhookInput').value.trim();
    if (!url) { showWebhookStatus('Please enter a webhook URL', 'error'); return; }
    saveSettings();
    showWebhookStatus('Sending test message...', '');
    try {
        const result = await fetch(url, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                embeds: [{
                    title: '✅ Grand Flip Out — Webhook Test',
                    description: 'Webhook is working perfectly! You will now receive dump/pump alerts.',
                    color: 0x22c55e,
                    fields: [
                        { name: 'Status', value: 'Connected', inline: true },
                        { name: 'Alerts', value: state.autoAlertsEnabled ? 'Enabled' : 'Disabled', inline: true }
                    ],
                    footer: { text: 'Grand Flip Out' },
                    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                }]
            })
        });
        if (result.ok) showWebhookStatus('✅ Test successful! Webhook is working.', 'success');
        else showWebhookStatus('❌ Webhook rejected (check URL)', 'error');
    } catch(e) {
        showWebhookStatus('❌ Failed to send: ' + e.message, 'error');
    }
}

function showWebhookStatus(msg, cls) {
    const status = document.getElementById('webhookStatus');
    status.textContent = msg;
    status.className = 'settings-status';
    if (cls) status.classList.add(cls);
}

async function sendDiscordAlert(item, type, percentChange) {
    if (!state.webhookUrl || !state.autoAlertsEnabled) return;
    if (type !== 'dump') return; // Only alert on dumps — pumps aren't actionable

    // Calculate the key numbers
    const buyAt = item.instaBuyAt || item.buyPrice;
    const sellFor = item.sellFor || item.sellPrice;
    const profitPerItem = item.flipProfit || (sellFor - buyAt - Math.min(Math.floor(sellFor * 0.02), 5000000));

    // ====== STRICT QUALITY FILTER ======
    // Only alert on dumps where someone can INSTA-BUY at buyAt and INSTA-SELL at sellFor
    // and walk away with real, meaningful profit. No tiny margins, no junk.

    // ====== DISCORD QUALITY BAR: ONLY EXCEPTIONAL DUMPS ======
    // Discord alerts should be rare and ALWAYS worth acting on.
    // If someone gets a ping, they should drop everything and go to the GE.

    // Minimum profit per item: 500K GP — must be a real opportunity
    if (profitPerItem < 500000) return;

    // Item must be worth at least 500K to flip
    if (buyAt < 500000) return;

    const vol5m = (item.buyQuantity || 0) + (item.sellQuantity || 0);
    if (vol5m < 5) return; // Must have real volume

    const vol4h = estimateVol4h(item.itemId, vol5m);
    const buyLimit = item.buyLimit || 999999;
    const amountToBuy = Math.min(vol4h, buyLimit);
    const totalProfit = profitPerItem * amountToBuy;

    // Total profit must be at least 3M to justify a Discord ping
    if (totalProfit < 3000000) return;

    // Use intelligent dump score — only alert on high-quality dumps
    const dumpScore = getDumpScore(item);
    if (dumpScore.score < 60) return;

    // ====== RATE LIMITING (persisted to localStorage so refreshes don't reset) ======
    const now = Date.now();

    // Load persisted rate limit state
    let rl = {};
    try { rl = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('gfo_discord_ratelimit') || '{}'); } catch {}
    if (!rl.perItem) rl.perItem = {};
    if (!rl.alerts) rl.alerts = [];

    // Clean old entries
    rl.alerts = rl.alerts.filter(t => (now - t) < 3600000);
    for (const [k, t] of Object.entries(rl.perItem)) {
        if ((now - t) > 3600000) delete rl.perItem[k];
    }

    // Per-item: 1 hour cooldown
    const key = `${item.itemId}`;
    if (rl.perItem[key] && (now - rl.perItem[key]) < 3600000) return;

    // Global: 1 alert per 15 MINUTES
    if (rl.lastGlobal && (now - rl.lastGlobal) < 900000) return;

    // Hourly cap: max 4 alerts per hour
    if (rl.alerts.length >= 4) return;

    // Save
    rl.perItem[key] = now;
    rl.lastGlobal = now;
    rl.alerts.push(now);
    try { localStorage.setItem('gfo_discord_ratelimit', JSON.stringify(rl)); } catch {}

    console.log(`[GFO] Discord alert: ${item.name} — ${gp(profitPerItem)}/item × ${amountToBuy} = ${gp(totalProfit)}`);

    // Discord = just the money. The smartness is in WHAT gets alerted, not the message.
    try {
        const resp = await fetch(state.webhookUrl, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                embeds: [{
                    title: `💰 ${item.name} — ${gp(profitPerItem)}/item`,
                    description: `Buy **${gp(buyAt)}** → Sell **${gp(sellFor)}** → **${gp(totalProfit)}** total`,
                    color: 0x22C55E,
                    thumbnail: item.icon ? { url: `https://oldschool.runescape.wiki/images/${encodeURIComponent(item.icon.replace(/ /g, '_'))}` } : undefined,
                    footer: { text: 'Grand Flip Out' },
                    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                }]
            })
        });
        if (!resp.ok) {
            console.error(`[GFO] Discord webhook failed: ${resp.status} ${resp.statusText}`);
        } else {
            console.log(`[GFO] Alert sent for ${item.name}`);
        }
    } catch(e) {
        console.error('[GFO] Discord webhook error:', e.message);
    }
}

function toggleNotifications(toggle) {
    if ('Notification' in window && Notification.permission === 'default') {
        Notification.requestPermission().then(p => {
            state.notificationsEnabled = p === 'granted';
            toggle.classList.toggle('on', state.notificationsEnabled);
            saveSettings();
        });
    } else if ('Notification' in window && Notification.permission === 'granted') {
        state.notificationsEnabled = !state.notificationsEnabled;
        toggle.classList.toggle('on');
        saveSettings();
    }
}

function toggleShowIntel(toggle) {
    state.showIntel = !state.showIntel;
    toggle.classList.toggle('on');
    saveSettings();
    renderTopFlips();
    renderSniperFeed();
}

function showDumpNotification(item) {
    if (!('Notification' in window) || Notification.permission !== 'granted') return;
    const profit = item.flipProfit || (item.sellPrice - item.buyPrice - Math.min(Math.floor(item.sellPrice * 0.02), 5000000));
    const n = new Notification(`💰 DUMP: ${item.name} — ${gp(profit)} profit`, {
        body: `Buy at ${gp(item.instaBuyAt || item.buyPrice)} → Sell for ${gp(item.sellFor || item.sellPrice)}`,
        icon: item.icon ? `https://oldschool.runescape.wiki/images/${encodeURIComponent(item.icon.replace(/ /g, '_'))}` : undefined,
        tag: `dump-${item.itemId}`,
        requireInteraction: false,
    });
    setTimeout(() => n.close(), 10000);
}

// ============================================
// JTI CALCULATOR
// ============================================
function calculateJTI(item) {
    const buyPrice = item.buyPrice || 0, sellPrice = item.sellPrice || 0;
    const buyVol = item.buyQuantity || 0, sellVol = item.sellQuantity || 0;
    const totalVol = buyVol + sellVol;
    const highTime = item.highTime || 0, lowTime = item.lowTime || 0;

    let freshness = 0;
    if (highTime || lowTime) {
        const age = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) - Math.max(highTime, lowTime);
        if (age < 30) freshness = 100; else if (age < 60) freshness = 95;
        else if (age < 120) freshness = 85; else if (age < 300) freshness = 70;
        else if (age < 600) freshness = 50; else if (age < 1200) freshness = 25;
        else freshness = Math.max(0, 100 - (age / 600) * 100);
    }
    let liquidity = 0;
    if (totalVol >= 100000) liquidity = 100; else if (totalVol >= 50000) liquidity = 90;
    else if (totalVol >= 10000) liquidity = 75; else if (totalVol >= 1000) liquidity = 50;
    else if (totalVol >= 100) liquidity = 25;
    else if (totalVol > 0) liquidity = Math.min(100, (totalVol / 100) * 25);
    let marginScore = 0;
    if (buyPrice > 0 && sellPrice > 0) {
        const spread = (sellPrice - buyPrice) / buyPrice;
        if (spread < 0) marginScore = 0; else if (spread === 0) marginScore = 20;
        else if (spread <= 0.025) marginScore = 40; else if (spread <= 0.05) marginScore = 100;
        else if (spread <= 0.10) marginScore = 80; else if (spread <= 0.20) marginScore = 50;
        else if (spread <= 0.40) marginScore = 25;
        else marginScore = Math.max(0, 100 - spread * 50);
    }
    let velocity = 0;
    if (totalVol >= 10000) velocity = 100; else if (totalVol >= 5000) velocity = 90;
    else if (totalVol >= 1000) velocity = 75; else if (totalVol >= 500) velocity = 60;
    else if (totalVol >= 100) velocity = 45; else if (totalVol >= 50) velocity = 30;
    else if (totalVol >= 10) velocity = 15;
    else if (totalVol > 0) velocity = Math.min(100, (totalVol / 10) * 15);
    const jti = Math.round((freshness*15 + liquidity*20 + marginScore*20 + 50*15 + 50*15 + velocity*15)/100);
    return Math.max(0, Math.min(100, jti));
}

// ============================================
// API
// ============================================
async function fetchBackend(ep) {
    try {
        const r = await fetch(`${state.apiUrl}${ep}`, { signal: AbortSignal.timeout(5000) });
        if (!r.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${r.status}`);
        return await r.json();
    } catch { return null; }
}
async function fetchWiki(ep) {
    try {
        const r = await fetch(`https://prices.runescape.wiki/api/v1/osrs${ep}`, {
            headers: {'User-Agent':'GrandFlipOut - OSRS Flipping Tool'},
            signal: AbortSignal.timeout(15000)
        });
        if (!r.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${r.status}`);
        return await r.json();
    } catch { return null; }
}

async function ensureMapping() {
    if (state.cachedMapping) return state.cachedMapping;
    const mapping = await fetchWiki('/mapping');
    if (!mapping) return null;
    const byId = {};
    mapping.forEach(i => { if (i && i.id) byId[i.id] = i; });
    state.cachedMapping = mapping;
    state.mappingById = byId;
    return mapping;
}

function processLatest(latestData, volData, force = false) {
    const items = [];
    let totalDrift = 0, priceCount = 0;
    for (const [idStr, pi] of Object.entries(latestData)) {
        const id = parseInt(idStr);
        if (!pi || !pi.high || !pi.low) continue;
        const meta = state.mappingById[id];
        if (!meta) continue;
        const bp = pi.low, sp = pi.high;
        const tax = Math.min(Math.floor(sp * 0.02), 5000000);
        const margin = sp - bp - tax;
        const mPct = bp > 0 ? ((margin / bp) * 100) : 0;
        const vi = volData[idStr] || {};
        const bv = vi.lowPriceVolume || 0, sv = vi.highPriceVolume || 0;
        const obj = {
            itemId:id, name:meta.name, icon:meta.icon,
            buyPrice:bp, sellPrice:sp, margin, marginPct:parseFloat(mPct.toFixed(1)),
            highTime:pi.highTime||0, lowTime:pi.lowTime||0,
            buyQuantity:bv, sellQuantity:sv, buyLimit:meta.limit||0, highAlch:meta.highalch||0,
        };
        obj.jtiScore = calculateJTI(obj);
        const prev = state.prevPrices[id], cur = Math.round((bp+sp)/2);
        if (prev && prev > 0) { obj.percentChange = ((cur-prev)/prev)*100; totalDrift += Math.abs(obj.percentChange); priceCount++; }
        else obj.percentChange = 0;
        state.prevPrices[id] = cur;
        if (margin > 0 && (bv+sv) > 0) items.push(obj);
    }
    items.sort((a,b) => realistic4hProfit(b) - realistic4hProfit(a));
    const avgDrift = priceCount > 0 ? totalDrift / priceCount : 100;
    return { items, significant: force || avgDrift > 0.5 || state.allItems.length === 0, avgDrift };
}

async function loadTopFlips(force = false) {
    // Try backend first but with a very short timeout (500ms) so we don't stall
    try {
        const r = await fetch(`${state.apiUrl}/api/items?sort=jti&limit=200`, { signal: AbortSignal.timeout(500) });
        if (r.ok) {
            const data = await r.json();
            if (data && data.items) {
                state.items = data.items.map(i => ({
                    itemId:i.itemId, name:i.name, icon:i.icon,
                    buyPrice:i.buyPrice, sellPrice:i.sellPrice,
                    margin:i.margin?.gp||i.margin||0, marginPct:i.margin?.percent?i.margin.percent.toFixed(1):0,
                    jtiScore:i.jti||0, buyQuantity:i.volume?.buy||0, sellQuantity:i.volume?.sell||0,
                    buyLimit:i.geLimit||0,
                }));
                state.allItems = [...state.items]; state.isConnected = true;
                updateStatus(true); renderAll(); return;
            }
        }
    } catch {}
    // Fall through to Wiki API (the primary data source)
    const mapping = await ensureMapping();
    if (!mapping) return;
    const [latest, vols] = await Promise.all([fetchWiki('/latest'), fetchWiki('/5m')]);
    if (!latest) return;
    const ld = latest.data||{}, vd = (vols&&vols.data)||{};
    state.cachedLatest = ld;
    state.cachedVolData = vd;
    const { items } = processLatest(ld, vd, force);
    state.allItems = items; state.items = items.slice(0, 200);
    state.isConnected = true; state.lastFullRefresh = Date.now();
    updateStatus(true);
    renderAll(); // Always render — never skip updates
}

// ============================================
// FETCH CACHING
// ============================================
async function fetchWikiCached(ep, maxAge = 5000) {
    const cached = state.fetchCache[ep];
    if (cached && (Date.now() - cached.time) < maxAge) return cached.data;
    const data = await fetchWiki(ep);
    if (data) state.fetchCache[ep] = { data, time: Date.now() };
    return data;
}

async function checkDumpsLight() {
    const [vols, latestResp, vol1h] = await Promise.all([
        fetchWikiCached('/5m', 5000),
        fetchWikiCached('/latest', 5000),
        fetchWikiCached('/1h', 5000)
    ]);
    if (!vols || !vols.data) return;

    // Always update latest prices for freshness
    if (latestResp && latestResp.data) {
        state.cachedLatest = latestResp.data;
    }
    let ld = state.cachedLatest;
    if (!ld) return;

    // Update volume data on existing items
    state.cachedVolData = vols.data;
    if (state.allItems.length > 0) {
        state.allItems.forEach(item => {
            const vi = vols.data[item.itemId];
            if (vi) {
                item.buyQuantity = vi.lowPriceVolume || 0;
                item.sellQuantity = vi.highPriceVolume || 0;
            }
        });
        state.items = state.allItems.slice(0, 200);
        renderTopFlips();
    }

    // ======= DUMP DETECTION: Find items you can BUY LOW and SELL HIGH right now =======
    // A "dump" = item price has crashed. You insta-buy at the crashed price, then sell at normal price.
    //
    // Key signals:
    //   - Insta-buy price (pi.low) = what you pay to buy the item RIGHT NOW
    //   - 1h average sell price (vi1h.avgHighPrice from /1h) = baseline for "normal" price
    //   - If insta-buy is much LOWER than 1h average → real crash → buy opportunity
    //   - Flip profit = sell price - buy price - 2% GE tax

    const nd = [], np = [];
    for (const [idStr, vi] of Object.entries(vols.data)) {
        const id = parseInt(idStr), meta = state.mappingById[id];
        if (!meta) continue;
        const pi = ld[idStr];
        if (!pi || !pi.high || !pi.low) continue;

        // Get 1h baseline for this item (smooth out noise)
        const vi1h = vol1h && vol1h.data ? vol1h.data[idStr] : null;

        // CORE PRICES for dump flipping:
        const instaBuyPrice = pi.low;    // What you pay to insta-buy RIGHT NOW
        const instaSellPrice = pi.high;   // What you get when you insta-sell RIGHT NOW
        const avgSellPrice5m = vi.avgHighPrice || 0;  // What items sold for recently (5m avg)
        const avgSellPrice1h = vi1h ? (vi1h.avgHighPrice || 0) : avgSellPrice5m;  // 1h average (better baseline)
        const avgBuyPrice5m = vi.avgLowPrice || 0;    // What items bought for recently (5m avg)
        const buyLimit = meta.limit || 0;

        const bv = vi.lowPriceVolume || 0, sv = vi.highPriceVolume || 0;
        if ((bv + sv) < 3) continue; // Need at least some volume

        // ====== ITEM QUALITY GATE ======
        // Use the NORMAL price (1h average) to judge item value, NOT current price.
        // A high-value item dumped to 1gp should STILL show up — that's the whole point.
        // But a bronze pickaxe that normally trades at 120gp? Always junk.

        const normalValue = avgSellPrice1h > 0 ? avgSellPrice1h : (avgSellPrice5m > 0 ? avgSellPrice5m : instaSellPrice);

        // 1. Item must normally be worth at least 50K GP
        //    This filters out bronze/iron/steel garbage, basic tools, quest junk
        //    But keeps expensive items that crash to low prices (that's a dump opportunity!)
        if (normalValue < 50000) continue;

        // 2. Name-based junk filter for items that are NEVER worth flipping
        //    regardless of price (novelty items, untradeable-adjacent junk)
        const nameLower = (meta.name || '').toLowerCase();
        const ALWAYS_JUNK = [
            'burnt ', 'broken ', 'damaged ',
            'cake tin', 'pie dish', 'beer glass',
            'wooden shield', 'leather body', 'leather chaps',
        ];
        if (ALWAYS_JUNK.some(p => nameLower.startsWith(p) || nameLower.includes(p))) continue;

        // THE DUMP FLIP: buy at instaBuyPrice, sell at instaSellPrice
        // Tax = 2% of sell price, capped at 5M
        const geTax = Math.min(Math.floor(instaSellPrice * 0.02), 5000000);
        const flipProfit = instaSellPrice - instaBuyPrice - geTax;

        // Use 1h average as baseline for crash detection (more accurate than 5m)
        let crashFromNormal = 0;
        const normalPrice = avgSellPrice1h > 0 ? avgSellPrice1h : avgSellPrice5m;
        if (normalPrice > 0 && instaBuyPrice > 0) {
            crashFromNormal = ((instaBuyPrice - normalPrice) / normalPrice) * 100;
        }

        // Also track 5m crash for compatibility
        let crashPct = 0;
        if (avgSellPrice5m > 0 && instaBuyPrice > 0) {
            crashPct = ((instaBuyPrice - avgSellPrice5m) / avgSellPrice5m) * 100;
        }

        // Also check: has the 5m avg BUY price dropped vs the latest trade?
        let buyDipPct = 0;
        if (avgBuyPrice5m > 0 && instaBuyPrice > 0) {
            buyDipPct = ((avgBuyPrice5m - instaBuyPrice) / instaBuyPrice) * 100;
        }

        // Track price history for trend analysis
        if (!state.priceHistory[id]) state.priceHistory[id] = [];
        const currentAvg = Math.round((instaBuyPrice + instaSellPrice) / 2);
        state.priceHistory[id].push({ time: Date.now(), price: currentAvg, vol: bv + sv });
        if (state.priceHistory[id].length > 10) state.priceHistory[id].shift();

        // Rolling trend: has this item been dropping over multiple checks?
        const history = state.priceHistory[id] || [];
        let trendPct = 0;
        if (history.length >= 3) {
            const oldest = history[0].price;
            const newest = history[history.length - 1].price;
            if (oldest > 0) trendPct = ((newest - oldest) / oldest) * 100;
        }

        // Volume pressure: more sellers than buyers = dump in progress
        const sellPressure = sv / Math.max(1, bv);
        const buyPressure = bv / Math.max(1, sv);

        // Margin percentage (how good is this flip?)
        const marginPct = instaBuyPrice > 0 ? (flipProfit / instaBuyPrice) * 100 : 0;

        // Store price baselines for this item
        state.priceBaselines[id] = { normal1h: avgSellPrice1h, normal5m: avgSellPrice5m, lastSeen: Date.now() };

        // DUMP SEVERITY: Better scoring using 1h baseline
        let severity = 0;
        if (crashFromNormal < -3) severity += Math.abs(crashFromNormal) * 1.5;  // Big crash from 1h normal
        if (crashFromNormal < -5) severity += 3;  // Extra bonus for 5%+ crashes
        if (trendPct < -2) severity += Math.abs(trendPct) * 0.5;  // Downward trend
        if (sellPressure > 2) severity += sellPressure * 0.5;  // Heavy selling
        if (flipProfit > 100000) severity += 2;  // Good profit opportunity
        if (flipProfit > 500000) severity += 3;  // Great profit opportunity
        if (flipProfit > 1000000) severity += 5;  // Huge profit opportunity
        if ((bv + sv) > 50) severity += 1;  // Liquid item

        const summary = {
            itemId: id, name: meta.name, icon: meta.icon,
            instaBuyAt: instaBuyPrice,    // "Buy NOW at this price"
            sellFor: instaSellPrice,       // "Then sell for this price"
            flipProfit: flipProfit,        // "You make this much per item"
            marginPct: marginPct,          // Margin as percentage
            crashPct: crashPct,            // How much it crashed (5m)
            crashFromNormal: crashFromNormal,  // How much below 1h normal
            // Keep old fields for compatibility
            buyPrice: instaBuyPrice, sellPrice: instaSellPrice,
            fiveMinAvg: avgSellPrice5m || currentAvg,
            percentChange: crashPct, trendPct: trendPct,
            buyQuantity: bv, sellQuantity: sv,
            buyLimit: buyLimit,
            severity: severity,
            sellPressure: sellPressure, buyPressure: buyPressure,
            highAlch: meta.highalch || 0
        };

        // Calculate dump score using the intelligent scoring engine
        const dumpScoreResult = getDumpScore(summary);
        summary.dumpScore = dumpScoreResult.score;

        // ====== VOLUME & DEMAND GATE ======
        // An item is only worth showing if people actually TRADE it
        // Low volume = you can't actually execute the flip = useless alert
        const totalVol5m = bv + sv;
        const estVolPerHour = totalVol5m * 12;
        const isHighDemand = estVolPerHour >= 20;       // 20+ trades/hr = decent liquidity
        const isMedDemand = estVolPerHour >= 8;          // 8+ trades/hr = tradeable
        const isLowDemand = estVolPerHour < 8;           // Under 8/hr = illiquid garbage

        // DUMP DETECTION: Use intelligent dump score with profit & demand gates
        const isDump = flipProfit >= 100000 && !isLowDemand && dumpScoreResult.score >= 35;

        // PUMP DETECTION: only items worth caring about
        // Use normalValue (not current price) so we catch pumps on valuable items
        const isPump = normalValue >= 50000 && isMedDemand && (
            (crashPct > 3 && normalValue >= 100000) ||
            (buyPressure > 3 && crashPct > 1 && normalValue >= 100000) ||
            (trendPct > 5 && isHighDemand && normalValue >= 100000)
        );

        if (isDump) nd.push(summary);
        if (isPump) np.push(summary);

        // Update prevPrices
        state.prevPrices[id] = currentAvg;
    }

    // Sort dumps by FLIP PROFIT (most profitable first!) — this is what matters
    nd.sort((a, b) => b.flipProfit - a.flipProfit);
    np.sort((a, b) => (b.sellPrice || 0) - (a.sellPrice || 0)); // Sort pumps by value, not %

    const prevDI = new Set(state.dumps.map(d=>d.itemId));
    const changed = nd.length !== state.dumps.length || nd.some(d => !prevDI.has(d.itemId));
    if (changed || np.length !== state.pumps.length) {
        state.dumps = nd.slice(0,15); state.pumps = np.slice(0,15);
        renderDumpsPumps();

        // Log new dumps
        const brandNew = nd.filter(d => !prevDI.has(d.itemId));
        brandNew.forEach(d => addDumpLog(d, 'dump'));
        np.forEach(p => {
            if (!new Set(state.dpHistory.flatMap(h => h.pumps || [])).has(p.itemId)) {
                addDumpLog(p, 'pump');
            }
        });

        // Discord alert: only the SINGLE best TRULY new dump
        // Use a persistent seen-set so items that flicker in/out don't re-trigger
        if (!state.discordAlertedItems) state.discordAlertedItems = {};
        const trulyNew = brandNew.filter(d => {
            const lastSeen = state.discordAlertedItems[d.itemId];
            // Consider "truly new" only if we haven't seen this item as a dump in the last 30 min
            return !lastSeen || (Date.now() - lastSeen) > 1800000;
        });
        if (trulyNew.length > 0) {
            const best = trulyNew[0]; // Already sorted by flipProfit desc
            state.discordAlertedItems[best.itemId] = Date.now();
            sendDiscordAlert(best, 'dump', 0);
        }
        // Cleanup old entries from seen-set
        const cutoff = Date.now() - 3600000;
        for (const [id, time] of Object.entries(state.discordAlertedItems)) {
            if (time < cutoff) delete state.discordAlertedItems[id];
        }

        // Browser notifications for high-profit dumps
        brandNew.filter(d => d.flipProfit >= 200000).forEach(d => showDumpNotification(d));
    }
    // Track history for chart
    state.dpHistory.push({ time: new Date(), dumps: nd.length, pumps: np.length });
    if (state.dpHistory.length > 60) state.dpHistory.shift();

    // Cleanup: remove price history for items not seen in 5 minutes
    const now = Date.now();
    for (const [id, history] of Object.entries(state.priceHistory)) {
        if (history.length > 0 && (now - history[history.length - 1].time) > 300000) {
            delete state.priceHistory[id];
        }
    }
}

// ============================================
// DUMP SCORING ENGINE
// ============================================
function getDumpScore(d) {
    let score = 0;
    const weights = {};

    // === PRICE SIGNALS (40% weight) ===
    // Crash from 1h normal — most reliable signal
    const crashNorm = Math.abs(d.crashFromNormal || 0);
    if (crashNorm > 10) score += 20;
    else if (crashNorm > 5) score += 15;
    else if (crashNorm > 3) score += 10;
    else if (crashNorm > 2) score += 5;
    weights.crashFromNormal = crashNorm;

    // Crash from 5m — short-term momentum
    const crash5m = Math.abs(d.crashPct || 0);
    if (crash5m > 5) score += 8;
    else if (crash5m > 2) score += 4;
    weights.crash5m = crash5m;

    // Price vs alch floor — items near alch floor can't drop much more (safer flip)
    if (d.highAlch && d.instaBuyAt) {
        const alchRatio = d.instaBuyAt / d.highAlch;
        if (alchRatio < 1.05) score += 8; // Near alch floor = safe
        else if (alchRatio < 1.15) score += 4;
    }

    // === VOLUME SIGNALS (25% weight) ===
    const volHr = ((d.buyQuantity || 0) + (d.sellQuantity || 0)) * 12;
    if (volHr > 200) score += 12;
    else if (volHr > 50) score += 8;
    else if (volHr > 20) score += 4;
    weights.volumeHr = volHr;

    // Sell pressure ratio — more sellers than buyers = dump in progress
    const sp = d.sellPressure || 0;
    if (sp > 4) score += 8;
    else if (sp > 2.5) score += 5;
    else if (sp > 1.5) score += 2;
    weights.sellPressure = sp;

    // === TREND SIGNALS (15% weight) ===
    const trend = d.trendPct || 0;
    if (trend < -5) score += 8;
    else if (trend < -3) score += 5;
    else if (trend < -1) score += 2;
    // Accelerating decline (trend worse than crash) = panic selling
    if (trend < d.crashPct && trend < -2) score += 5;
    weights.trend = trend;

    // === PROFIT SIGNALS (15% weight) ===
    const profit = d.flipProfit || 0;
    if (profit > 1000000) score += 10;
    else if (profit > 500000) score += 7;
    else if (profit > 200000) score += 4;
    else if (profit > 100000) score += 2;
    weights.profit = profit;

    // === MANIPULATION DETECTION (penalty) ===
    // If margin is suspiciously high (>20%) with low volume, likely stale/manipulated
    const marginPct = d.marginPct || 0;
    if (marginPct > 20 && volHr < 20) score -= 15;
    // If buy and sell quantities are nearly identical and very low, could be wash trading
    const bq = d.buyQuantity || 0, sq = d.sellQuantity || 0;
    if (bq > 0 && sq > 0 && Math.abs(bq - sq) <= 1 && (bq + sq) < 6) score -= 10;
    // Price seems too good to be true — massive margin on expensive item with no volume
    if (profit > 5000000 && volHr < 10) score -= 20;

    // === RECOVERY PROBABILITY ===
    // Items near alch floor almost always recover
    // Items with high base demand (consumables, BIS gear) recover faster
    // Items being dumped by bots may NOT recover
    let recoveryBonus = 0;
    if (d.highAlch && d.instaBuyAt && d.instaBuyAt < d.highAlch * 1.1) recoveryBonus += 5;
    if (volHr > 100) recoveryBonus += 3; // Liquid items recover faster
    if (sp > 4 && trend < -5) recoveryBonus -= 5; // Panic selling = may keep going down
    score += recoveryBonus;

    // === TIME-OF-DAY ADJUSTMENT ===
    const hour = new Date().getHours();
    const isDeadHours = hour >= 2 && hour <= 7; // 2am-7am = low activity
    const isPeakHours = hour >= 17 && hour <= 23; // 5pm-11pm = peak
    if (isDeadHours) {
        // During dead hours, prices are more volatile but less reliable
        // Crashes during dead hours are often just low liquidity, not real dumps
        if (volHr < 30) score -= 10;
    }
    if (isPeakHours) {
        // During peak hours, high-volume crashes are more meaningful
        if (volHr > 100 && crashNorm > 3) score += 5;
    }
    weights.timeOfDay = isPeakHours ? 'peak' : isDeadHours ? 'dead' : 'normal';

    // === ITEM CATEGORY BONUSES ===
    const name = (d.name || '').toLowerCase();
    // PvM BIS gear always has demand — dumps are real opportunities
    const isPvmBis = ['twisted bow', 'scythe', 'rapier', 'avernic', 'torva', 'masori',
        'ancestral', 'kodai', 'harmonised', 'eldritch', 'volatile', 'inquisitor',
        'dragon hunter', 'dragon warhammer', 'primordial', 'pegasian', 'eternal',
        'bandos', 'armadyl', 'saradomin sword', 'zamorakian spear',
        'oathplate', 'virtus', 'bellator', 'venator', 'ultor', 'magus',
        'tumeken', 'osmumten', 'lightbearer', 'elidinis',
        'necklace of anguish', 'amulet of torture', 'tormented bracelet',
        'bow of faerdhinen', 'blade of saeldor', 'eclipse'].some(p => name.includes(p));
    if (isPvmBis) score += 8;

    // Consumables always have demand — very safe flips
    const isConsumable = ['potion', 'brew', 'restore', 'prayer', 'stamina',
        'anglerfish', 'manta ray', 'dark crab', 'shark', 'karambwan',
        'cannonball', 'dragon dart', 'rune arrow', 'amethyst arrow',
        'blood rune', 'death rune', 'soul rune', 'wrath rune',
        'zulrah scale', 'divine'].some(p => name.includes(p));
    if (isConsumable && volHr > 50) score += 5;

    // Bot-farmed items: crashes are often NOT recoverable (just more bots)
    const isBotItem = ['yew log', 'magic log', 'gold ore', 'iron ore', 'coal',
        'green dragonhide', 'flax', 'bow string', 'nature rune',
        'grimy guam', 'grimy tarromin', 'grimy harralander', 'grimy marrentill',
        'black chinchompa', 'red chinchompa', 'amylase'].some(p => name.includes(p));
    if (isBotItem) score -= 5; // Bot items: crashes may not recover

    return {
        score: Math.max(0, Math.min(100, score)),
        weights,
        isPvmBis, isConsumable, isBotItem,
        recoveryLikely: recoveryBonus > 0,
        isDeadHours, isPeakHours
    };
}

function addDumpLog(item, type) {
    const profit = item.flipProfit || (item.sellPrice - item.buyPrice - Math.min(Math.floor(item.sellPrice * 0.02), 5000000));
    state.dumpLog.push({
        time: new Date(),
        itemId: item.itemId,
        name: item.name,
        icon: item.icon,
        percentChange: item.percentChange,
        flipProfit: profit,
        buyPrice: item.instaBuyAt || item.buyPrice,
        sellPrice: item.sellFor || item.sellPrice,
        type: type
    });
    if (state.dumpLog.length > 100) state.dumpLog.shift();
    renderDumpLog();
}

function renderDumpLog() {
    const container = document.getElementById('dumpLogBody');
    if (!container) return;
    if (state.dumpLog.length === 0) {
        container.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center; color:var(--text-muted); padding:16px; font-size:12px;">Logs will appear here...</div>';
        return;
    }
    container.innerHTML = state.dumpLog.slice().reverse().map(entry => {
        const profitDisplay = entry.flipProfit ? gp(Math.abs(entry.flipProfit)) : gp(0);
        const profitColor = entry.type === 'dump' ? 'var(--green)' : 'var(--accent)';
        const profitLabel = entry.type === 'dump' ? `+${profitDisplay}/item` : `${gp(entry.sellPrice || 0)}`;
        return `
        <div class="dumplog-entry">
            <div class="dumplog-entry-icon">${iconHtml(entry.icon, entry.name, 28)}</div>
            <div class="dumplog-entry-info">
                <div class="dumplog-entry-name">${entry.name}</div>
                <div style="display: flex; gap: 8px; align-items: center;">
                    <span style="color:${profitColor}; font-weight:700; font-size:12px;">${profitLabel}</span>
                    <span class="dumplog-entry-type ${entry.type}">${entry.type}</span>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="dumplog-entry-time">${entry.time.toLocaleTimeString([], {hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit',second:'2-digit'})}</div>
        </div>`;
    }).join('');
}

async function loadDumpsPumps() {
    const d = await fetchBackend('/api/dumps');
    if (d && d.dumps) {
        state.dumps = d.dumps.map(x => ({ itemId:x.itemId, name:x.itemName||x.name||'?', buyPrice:x.buyPrice||0, sellPrice:x.sellPrice||0, percentChange:x.percentChange||0 }));
        renderDumpsPumps(); return;
    }
    await checkDumpsLight();
}

async function loadRecipes() {
    let data = await fetchBackend('/api/recipes');
    if (data && data.recipes) { state.recipes = data.recipes; renderRecipes(); return; }
    const knownRecipes = []; let idC = 1;
    try {
        const jr = await fetch('./data/recipes.json').then(r => r.ok ? r.json() : null);
        if (jr) {
            (jr.herbCleaning||[]).forEach(h => knownRecipes.push({ id:idC++, name:`Clean ${h.herb}`, type:'herb-cleaning', input:`Grimy ${h.herb}`, output:h.herb, rawId:h.rawId, processedId:h.processedId, skill:'Herblore', level:h.level, experience:h.experience, inputPrice:0, outputPrice:0, profit:0 }));
            (jr.gemCutting||[]).forEach(g => knownRecipes.push({ id:idC++, name:`Cut ${g.gem}`, type:'gem-cutting', input:`Uncut ${g.gem}`, output:g.gem, rawId:g.rawId, processedId:g.processedId, skill:'Crafting', level:g.level, experience:g.experience, inputPrice:0, outputPrice:0, profit:0 }));
            (jr.smelting||[]).forEach(s => knownRecipes.push({ id:idC++, name:s.name, type:'smelting', input:s.name.split(' -> ')[0]||'', output:s.name.split(' -> ')[1]||'', rawId:s.rawId, processedId:s.processedId, skill:'Smithing', level:s.level, experience:s.experience, inputPrice:0, outputPrice:0, profit:0 }));
        }
    } catch {}
    data = await autoDiscoverRecipes(knownRecipes, idC);
    if (data && data.length > 0) {
        let ld = {};
        if (state.allItems.length > 0) state.allItems.forEach(i => { ld[i.itemId] = { low:i.buyPrice, high:i.sellPrice }; });
        else { const l = await fetchWiki('/latest'); if (l && l.data) ld = l.data; }
        data.forEach(r => {
            const ip = ld[r.rawId], op = ld[r.processedId];
            if (ip) r.inputPrice = ip.low || ip.high || 0;
            if (op) r.outputPrice = op.high || op.low || 0;
            r.profit = r.outputPrice - r.inputPrice;
        });
        data = data.filter(r => r.profit > 0).sort((a,b) => b.profit - a.profit);
    }
    state.recipes = data || [];
    renderRecipes();
}

async function autoDiscoverRecipes(known, startId) {
    try {
        const mapping = state.cachedMapping || await fetchWiki('/mapping');
        if (!mapping) return known;
        const byName = new Map();
        mapping.forEach(i => { if (i && i.name) { const l = i.name.toLowerCase(); if (!byName.has(l)) byName.set(l, []); byName.get(l).push(i); }});
        let idC = startId, existing = new Set(known.map(r => r.rawId).filter(Boolean)), disc = 0;
        const patterns = [
            { regex: /^Grimy\s+(.+)$/i, type:'herb-cleaning', skill:'Herblore', prefix:'Clean' },
            { regex: /^Uncut\s+(.+)$/i, type:'gem-cutting', skill:'Crafting', prefix:'Cut' },
            { regex: /^Raw\s+(.+)$/i, type:'cooking', skill:'Cooking', prefix:'Cook' },
        ];
        for (const p of patterns) {
            mapping.forEach(item => {
                if (existing.has(item.id)) return;
                const m = item.name.match(p.regex);
                if (m) {
                    const matches = byName.get(m[1].toLowerCase());
                    if (matches && matches.length > 0) {
                        known.push({ id:idC++, name:`${p.prefix} ${m[1]} (Auto)`, type:p.type, input:item.name, output:matches[0].name, rawId:item.id, processedId:matches[0].id, skill:p.skill, level:1, experience:0, inputPrice:0, outputPrice:0, profit:0, autoDiscovered:true });
                        existing.add(item.id); disc++;
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        return known;
    } catch { return known; }
}

// ============================================
// HELPERS
// ============================================
function gp(v) { if (!v) return '0 gp'; const a = Math.abs(v); if (a >= 1000000) return (v/1000000).toFixed(1) + 'M'; if (a >= 1000) return (v/1000).toFixed(1) + 'K'; return v.toLocaleString() + ' gp'; }
function gpFull(v) { return v ? Math.abs(v).toLocaleString() + ' gp' : '0 gp'; }

function volPerHour(item) { return (item.buyQuantity + item.sellQuantity) * 12; }
// Smarter volume estimation using rolling average from price history
function estimateVol4h(itemId, current5mVol) {
    const history = state.priceHistory[itemId] || [];
    if (history.length < 3) {
        // Not enough data, use conservative estimate
        return Math.round(current5mVol * 12 * 4 * 0.5); // 50% haircut
    }
    // Average volume across all snapshots
    const avgVol = history.reduce((sum, h) => sum + h.vol, 0) / history.length;
    // Use the LOWER of current and average (conservative)
    const conservativeVol = Math.min(current5mVol, avgVol);
    return Math.round(conservativeVol * 12 * 4);
}
function realisticBuys(item) {
    const vol4h = estimateVol4h(item.itemId, item.buyQuantity + item.sellQuantity);
    const limit = item.buyLimit || 999999;
    return Math.min(limit, Math.floor(vol4h));
}
function realistic4hProfit(item) { return item.margin * realisticBuys(item); }
// Hash function for rendering optimization
function itemsHash(items) {
    return items.slice(0, 20).map(i => `${i.itemId}:${i.buyPrice}:${i.sellPrice}`).join('|');
}

function getVerdict(item) {
    const vph = volPerHour(item);
    const profit4h = realistic4hProfit(item);
    const margin = item.margin || 0;
    if (vph < 12) return { text:'Dead', cls:'dead', tip:'Almost no one is trading this' };
    if (vph < 60 || profit4h < 10000) return { text:'Slow', cls:'slow', tip:'Low activity — small profits' };
    if (profit4h < 100000 || vph < 200) return { text:'Decent', cls:'decent', tip:'Okay flip — moderate volume' };
    if (profit4h < 500000) return { text:'Good Flip', cls:'good', tip:'Solid margins with real volume' };
    return { text:'Great Flip', cls:'great', tip:'High profit with strong volume' };
}
function formatVolPerHour(item) {
    const vph = volPerHour(item);
    if (vph === 0) return 'None';
    if (vph < 12) return '<12/hr';
    if (vph >= 10000) return (vph/1000).toFixed(0) + 'K/hr';
    if (vph >= 1000) return (vph/1000).toFixed(1) + 'K/hr';
    return '~' + vph.toLocaleString() + '/hr';
}

          reason: 'DKS rings. Heavily farmed but consistent demand. Imbued versions are BiS — unimbued prices track imbue scroll supply.' },

        // THIEVING BOT SUPPLY
        { match: ['dragonstone', 'uncut dragonstone'], tag: 'bot-supply', icon: '💎',
          reason: 'Rogues Castle thieving bots dump dragonstones from chests. Level 84 Thieving bots flood supply in Wilderness.' },

        // HIGH-DEMAND TRAINING SUPPLIES
        { match: ['dragon dart', 'dragon dart tip'], tag: 'consumable', icon: '🎯',
          reason: 'BiS ammo for blowpipe. Consumed rapidly in PvM. Supply from Volcanic Mine and Vorkath. Price tracks demand cycles.' },
        { match: ['anglerfish', 'cooked anglerfish'], tag: 'consumable', icon: '🐟',
          reason: 'Best food for PvM/PvP (heals above max HP). Piscarilius fishing supplies the market. Steady demand.' },
        { match: ['dark crab', 'cooked dark crab'], tag: 'consumable', icon: '🦀',
          reason: 'Wilderness-only food. Supply limited by location risk. Prices volatile around PvP activity changes.' },
        { match: ['manta ray', 'cooked manta ray'], tag: 'consumable', icon: '🐟',
          reason: 'Top-tier food. Steady PvM demand. Supply from Tempoross and fishing. Reliable flip item.' },
    ],
    // Dynamic intel based on item data
    getDynamic(item) {
        const insights = [];
        const vph = volPerHour(item);
        const margin = item.margin || 0;
        const mPct = item.marginPct || 0;

        // Alch value insight
        if (item.highAlch && item.buyPrice) {
            const alchProfit = item.highAlch - item.buyPrice - 200;
            if (alchProfit > 0 && alchProfit > margin) {
                insights.push({ icon: '🔥', text: `Can alch for ${gp(alchProfit)} profit instead of flipping`, tag: 'alch-floor' });
            }
            if (item.buyPrice < item.highAlch * 1.02) {
                insights.push({ icon: '🛡️', text: `Near alch floor — price can't drop much further`, tag: 'alch-floor' });
            }
        }

        // Volume insight
        if (vph > 5000) {
            insights.push({ icon: '🌊', text: 'Very liquid — fills fast', tag: 'volume' });
        } else if (vph < 24) {
            insights.push({ icon: '⚠️', text: 'Low volume — slow fills', tag: 'volume' });
        }

        // Margin insight
        if (mPct > 15) {
            insights.push({ icon: '🚩', text: 'Unusually high margin — could be stale data or manipulation', tag: 'warning' });
        }

        // Buy limit constraint
        if (item.buyLimit && item.buyLimit < 50 && margin > 50000) {
            insights.push({ icon: '🔒', text: `Buy limit ${item.buyLimit} — max ${gp(margin * item.buyLimit)} per 4h`, tag: 'volume' });
        }

        // Item sink awareness (GE tax removes 2% of all traded items)
        if (item.buyPrice > 5000000) {
            insights.push({ icon: '📉', text: 'GE item sink is slowly reducing supply — long-term price support', tag: 'alch-floor' });
        }

        return insights;
    },
    // Get all intel for an item
    getIntel(item) {
        const name = (item.name || '').toLowerCase();
        const results = [];

        // Check static rules
        for (const rule of this.rules) {
            if (rule.match.some(m => name.includes(m.toLowerCase()))) {
                results.push({ icon: rule.icon, text: rule.reason, tag: rule.tag });
            }
        }

        // Add dynamic insights
        results.push(...this.getDynamic(item));

        return results;
    }
};

function iconUrl(icon) { return icon ? `https://oldschool.runescape.wiki/images/${encodeURIComponent(icon.replace(/ /g,'_'))}` : ''; }
function iconHtml(icon, name, size=32) {
    if (!icon) return `<div style="width:${size}px;height:${size}px;display:grid;place-items:center;font-size:${size*0.6}px;color:var(--gold);">$</div>`;
    return `<img src="${iconUrl(icon)}" alt="${name||''}" style="width:${size}px;height:${size}px;object-fit:contain;" onerror="this.outerHTML='<div style=\\'width:${size}px;height:${size}px;display:grid;place-items:center;font-size:${size*0.6}px;color:var(--gold);\\'>$</div>'">`;
}
function updateStatus(on) {
    document.getElementById('statusDot').className = 'status-dot ' + (on ? 'on' : 'off');
    document.getElementById('statusText').textContent = on ? 'Live' : 'Offline';
    const now = new Date();
    document.getElementById('lastUpdate').textContent = now.toLocaleTimeString([], {hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit',second:'2-digit'});
    state.lastUpdate = now;
}

function openOSRSWiki(itemName) {
    const url = `https://oldschool.runescape.wiki/w/${encodeURIComponent(itemName.replace(/ /g, '_'))}`;
    window.open(url, '_blank');
}

let _refreshing = false;
async function manualRefresh() {
    if (_refreshing) return;
    _refreshing = true;
    const pill = document.getElementById('statusPill');
    const text = document.getElementById('statusText');
    pill.classList.add('refreshing');
    text.textContent = 'Refreshing...';
    try {
        await loadTopFlips(true);
        await checkDumpsLight();
        await loadRecipes();
        text.textContent = 'Live';
        state.refreshCountdown = Math.floor(state.fullRefreshInterval / 1000);
    } catch(e) {
        text.textContent = 'Error';
        setTimeout(() => { text.textContent = state.isConnected ? 'Live' : 'Offline'; }, 2000);
    }
    pill.classList.remove('refreshing');
    _refreshing = false;
}

// ============================================
// COUNTDOWN TIMER
// ============================================
function startCountdownTimer() {
    state.refreshCountdown = Math.floor(state.fullRefreshInterval / 1000);
    const timerEl = document.getElementById('countdownTimer');

    const interval = setInterval(() => {
        state.refreshCountdown--;
        if (state.refreshCountdown <= 0) {
            clearInterval(interval);
            timerEl.textContent = '';
        } else if (state.refreshCountdown > 0) {
            timerEl.textContent = `Next: ${state.refreshCountdown}s`;
        }
    }, 1000);
}

// ============================================
// SCROLL TO TOP VISIBILITY
// ============================================
document.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
    const scrollBtn = document.getElementById('scrollToTop');
    if (window.scrollY > 300) {
        scrollBtn.classList.add('show');
    } else {
        scrollBtn.classList.remove('show');
    }
});

// ============================================
// RENDERING
// ============================================
function renderAll() {
    renderDashboard();
    renderTopFlips();
    renderDumpsPumps();
    renderWatchlist();
}

function renderDashboard() {
    const items = state.allItems;
    document.getElementById('statItems').textContent = items.length.toLocaleString();
    if (items.length > 0) {
        const best = items.reduce((a,b) => realistic4hProfit(b) > realistic4hProfit(a) ? b : a, items[0]);
        const rp = realistic4hProfit(best);
        document.getElementById('statBestProfit').textContent = gp(rp) + '/4h';
        document.getElementById('statBestName').textContent = best.name + ' (' + gp(best.margin) + '/item)';
    }
    document.getElementById('statDumps').textContent = state.dumps.length;
    document.getElementById('statPumps').textContent = state.pumps.length;
    renderCharts();
}

function renderCharts() {
    const items = state.allItems;
    if (items.length === 0) return;

    const top10rp = [...items].sort((a,b) => realistic4hProfit(b) - realistic4hProfit(a)).slice(0,10);
    updateChart('chartMargins', 'bar', {
        labels: top10rp.map(i => i.name.length > 15 ? i.name.slice(0,14)+'...' : i.name),
        datasets: [{ label:'4h Profit', data:top10rp.map(i => realistic4hProfit(i)), backgroundColor:'rgba(34,197,94,0.7)', borderColor:'#22c55e', borderWidth:1, borderRadius:4 }]
    }, { indexAxis:'y', plugins:{legend:{display:false}}, scales:{ x:{ticks:{color:'#7a7268',callback:v=>gp(v)},grid:{color:'rgba(255,152,31,0.08)'}}, y:{ticks:{color:'#b8b0a5',font:{size:11}},grid:{display:false}} }});

    const verdictCounts = { 'Great Flip':0, 'Good Flip':0, 'Decent':0, 'Slow':0, 'Dead':0 };
    items.forEach(i => { const v = getVerdict(i); verdictCounts[v.text] = (verdictCounts[v.text]||0) + 1; });
    updateChart('chartJtiDist', 'doughnut', {
        labels: Object.keys(verdictCounts),
        datasets: [{ data:Object.values(verdictCounts), backgroundColor:['#22c55e','#4ade80','#ff981f','#d97706','#ef4444'], borderWidth:0 }]
    }, { plugins:{legend:{position:'right',labels:{color:'#b8b0a5',font:{size:11},padding:8}}} });

    const top10v = [...items].sort((a,b) => volPerHour(b) - volPerHour(a)).slice(0,10);
    updateChart('chartVolume', 'bar', {
        labels: top10v.map(i => i.name.length > 15 ? i.name.slice(0,14)+'...' : i.name),
        datasets: [
            { label:'Buy Vol/hr', data:top10v.map(i=>i.buyQuantity*12), backgroundColor:'rgba(34,197,94,0.6)', borderRadius:4 },
            { label:'Sell Vol/hr', data:top10v.map(i=>i.sellQuantity*12), backgroundColor:'rgba(239,68,68,0.6)', borderRadius:4 },
        ]
    }, { indexAxis:'y', plugins:{legend:{labels:{color:'#b8b0a5'}}}, scales:{ x:{stacked:true,ticks:{color:'#7a7268'},grid:{color:'rgba(255,152,31,0.08)'}}, y:{stacked:true,ticks:{color:'#b8b0a5',font:{size:11}},grid:{display:false}} }});

    const top50 = items.slice(0, 50);
    updateChart('chartScatter', 'scatter', {
        datasets: [{ label:'Items', data: top50.map(i => ({ x:volPerHour(i), y:Math.round(i.margin/1000), name:i.name })),
            backgroundColor:'rgba(255,152,31,0.5)', borderColor:'#ff981f', pointRadius:5, pointHoverRadius:8 }]
    }, { plugins:{legend:{display:false},tooltip:{callbacks:{label:ctx=>`${ctx.raw.name}: ${gp(ctx.raw.y*1000)}/item, ~${ctx.raw.x}/hr`}}}, scales:{ x:{title:{display:true,text:'Volume per Hour (est.)',color:'#7a7268'},ticks:{color:'#7a7268'},grid:{color:'rgba(255,152,31,0.08)'}}, y:{title:{display:true,text:'Profit/Item (K GP)',color:'#7a7268'},ticks:{color:'#7a7268',callback:v=>gp(v*1000)},grid:{color:'rgba(255,152,31,0.08)'}} }});
}

function updateChart(canvasId, type, data, options) {
    const ctx = document.getElementById(canvasId);
    if (!ctx) return;
    if (state.charts[canvasId]) { state.charts[canvasId].destroy(); }
    state.charts[canvasId] = new Chart(ctx, { type, data, options: { responsive:true, maintainAspectRatio:false, animation:{duration:400}, ...options } });
}

function renderSniperFeed() {
    const feed = document.getElementById('sniperFeed');
    if (!feed) return;

    const dumps = state.dumps;

    // Update sniper stats
    const targetsEl = document.getElementById('sniperTargets');
    const maxSevEl = document.getElementById('sniperMaxCrash');
    const bestOppEl = document.getElementById('sniperBestOpp');
    const bestNameEl = document.getElementById('sniperBestName');
    const badgeEl = document.getElementById('sniperBadge');

    if (targetsEl) targetsEl.textContent = dumps.length;
    // Badge shows high-quality dumps only (strong dump score)
    const highConfDumps = dumps.filter(d => getDumpScore(d).score >= 70);
    if (badgeEl) badgeEl.textContent = highConfDumps.length > 0 ? highConfDumps.length : '';

    if (dumps.length > 0) {
        // Show the best total profit opportunity (real money, real number)
        const bestTotal = Math.max(...dumps.map(d => {
            const p = d.flipProfit || (d.sellPrice - d.buyPrice - Math.min(Math.floor(d.sellPrice * 0.02), 5000000));
            const v4h = Math.round((d.buyQuantity + d.sellQuantity) * 12 * 4);
            const lim = d.buyLimit || 999999;
            return p * Math.min(v4h, lim);
        }));
        if (maxSevEl) maxSevEl.textContent = gp(bestTotal);

        // Best opportunity: dump with best FLIP PROFIT
        const sorted = [...dumps].sort((a, b) => (b.flipProfit || 0) - (a.flipProfit || 0));
        const best = sorted[0];

        if (best && bestOppEl) {
            const profit = best.flipProfit || (best.sellPrice - best.buyPrice - Math.min(Math.floor(best.sellPrice * 0.02), 5000000));
            bestOppEl.textContent = gp(profit) + '/item';
            if (bestNameEl) bestNameEl.textContent = best.name;
        }
    } else {
        if (maxSevEl) maxSevEl.textContent = '—';
        if (bestOppEl) bestOppEl.textContent = '—';
        if (bestNameEl) bestNameEl.textContent = 'scanning...';
    }

    if (dumps.length === 0) {
        feed.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-icon">🎯</div><p>No dumps detected — market looks stable. Scanning every 8 seconds...</p></div>';
        return;
    }

    feed.innerHTML = dumps.map(d => {
        const profit = d.flipProfit || (d.sellPrice - d.buyPrice - Math.min(Math.floor(d.sellPrice * 0.02), 5000000));

        // Calculate what you can actually buy
        const vol4h = Math.round((d.buyQuantity + d.sellQuantity) * 12 * 4);
        const buyLimit = d.buyLimit || 999999;
        const canBuy = Math.min(vol4h, buyLimit);
        const totalProfit = profit * canBuy;

        // SMART CONTEXT: translate framework intelligence into plain English
        const tags = [];
        // Speed/urgency signal
        if (d.sellPressure > 3) tags.push({ text: 'Heavy selling', color: 'var(--red)', icon: '🔴' });
        else if (d.sellPressure > 1.8) tags.push({ text: 'Sellers flooding', color: 'var(--accent)', icon: '🟠' });
        // Trend signal
        if (d.trendPct && d.trendPct < -3) tags.push({ text: 'Still dropping', color: 'var(--red)', icon: '📉' });
        else if (d.crashFromNormal && d.crashFromNormal < -5) tags.push({ text: 'Way below normal', color: 'var(--green)', icon: '💎' });
        else if (d.crashFromNormal && d.crashFromNormal < -3) tags.push({ text: 'Below normal', color: 'var(--green)', icon: '✅' });
        // Volume signal
        const volHr = (d.buyQuantity + d.sellQuantity) * 12;
        if (volHr > 100) tags.push({ text: 'Very liquid', color: 'var(--blue)', icon: '💧' });
        else if (volHr < 15) tags.push({ text: 'Low volume', color: 'var(--text-muted)', icon: '⚠️' });
        // Market intel
        const intel = MARKET_INTEL.getIntel(d);
        if (intel.length > 0) tags.push({ text: intel[0].text.length > 25 ? intel[0].text.slice(0,24) + '…' : intel[0].text, color: 'var(--accent)', icon: intel[0].icon });

        const tagsHtml = tags.length > 0 ? `<div style="display:flex; gap:4px; flex-wrap:wrap; margin-top:6px;">${tags.slice(0,3).map(t => `<span style="font-size:10px; padding:2px 6px; border-radius:4px; background:rgba(255,255,255,0.05); border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.08); color:${t.color};">${t.icon} ${t.text}</span>`).join('')}</div>` : '';

        const buyLimitHtml = buyLimit < 100 ? `<span style="margin-left:6px; color:var(--red); font-weight:700; font-size:10px;">⚠️ Limit: ${buyLimit}</span>` : '';

        return `
        <div class="dp-section" style="padding:16px; cursor:pointer; border-left:4px solid ${profit >= 300000 ? 'var(--green)' : profit > 0 ? 'var(--accent)' : 'var(--red)'};" onclick="openOSRSWiki('${d.name.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">
            <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:12px; margin-bottom:12px;">
                <div class="dp-item-icon" style="width:44px;height:44px;">${iconHtml(d.icon, d.name, 44)}</div>
                <div style="flex:1;">
                    <div style="font-weight:700; font-size:16px; color:var(--text);">${d.name}${buyLimitHtml}</div>${tagsHtml}
                </div>
                <div style="text-align:right;">
                    <div style="font-size:22px; font-weight:900; color:var(--green); text-shadow:0 0 12px rgba(34,197,94,0.3);">${gp(profit)}<span style="font-size:11px; font-weight:500; color:var(--text-muted);">/item</span></div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div style="display:flex; gap:0; margin-bottom:10px; background:rgba(0,0,0,0.3); border-radius:8px; overflow:hidden;">
                <div style="flex:1; padding:10px 12px; text-align:center; border-right:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.05);">
                    <div style="font-size:9px; text-transform:uppercase; color:var(--green); letter-spacing:.5px; font-weight:600;">Buy At</div>
                    <div style="font-size:18px; font-weight:900; color:var(--green); margin-top:4px;">${gp(d.instaBuyAt || d.buyPrice)}</div>
                </div>
                <div style="flex:1; padding:10px 12px; text-align:center; border-right:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.05);">
                    <div style="font-size:9px; text-transform:uppercase; color:var(--text-muted); letter-spacing:.5px; font-weight:600;">Buy</div>
                    <div style="font-size:18px; font-weight:900; color:var(--text); margin-top:4px;">${canBuy.toLocaleString()}</div>
                </div>
                <div style="flex:1; padding:10px 12px; text-align:center;">
                    <div style="font-size:9px; text-transform:uppercase; color:var(--accent); letter-spacing:.5px; font-weight:600;">Sell For</div>
                    <div style="font-size:18px; font-weight:900; color:var(--accent); margin-top:4px;">${gp(d.sellFor || d.sellPrice)}</div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div style="background:rgba(34,197,94,0.12); border:1px solid rgba(34,197,94,0.25); border-radius:8px; padding:10px; text-align:center;">
                <span style="font-size:11px; color:var(--text-muted);">Total Profit: </span>
                <span style="font-size:18px; font-weight:900; color:var(--green);">${gp(totalProfit)}</span>
                ${d.buyLimit && d.buyLimit < vol4h ? `<span style="font-size:10px; color:var(--text-muted); margin-left:8px;">(GE limit: ${d.buyLimit.toLocaleString()})</span>` : ''}
            </div>
        </div>`;
    }).join('');

    // Render sniper charts
    renderSniperCharts(dumps);
}

function renderSniperCharts(dumps) {
    if (dumps.length > 0) {
        const top8 = [...dumps].sort((a,b) => (b.flipProfit||0) - (a.flipProfit||0)).slice(0, 8);
        updateChart('chartSniperOpp', 'bar', {
            labels: top8.map(d => d.name.length > 14 ? d.name.slice(0,13)+'...' : d.name),
            datasets: [
                { label: 'Flip Profit (K)', data: top8.map(d => Math.round((d.flipProfit || 0) / 1000)), backgroundColor: 'rgba(34,197,94,0.6)', borderRadius: 4 },
                { label: 'Profit/Item (K)', data: top8.map(d => Math.round((d.flipProfit || 0) / 1000)), backgroundColor: 'rgba(34,197,94,0.6)', borderRadius: 4 },
            ]
        }, { indexAxis:'y', plugins:{legend:{labels:{color:'#b8b0a5'}}}, scales:{ x:{ticks:{color:'#7a7268'},grid:{color:'rgba(255,152,31,0.08)'}}, y:{ticks:{color:'#b8b0a5',font:{size:11}},grid:{display:false}} }});
    }

    // Severity over time chart
    if (!state.sniperHistory) state.sniperHistory = [];
    const bestProfit = state.dumps.length > 0 ? Math.max(...state.dumps.map(d => (d.flipProfit || 0) / 1000)) : 0;
    state.sniperHistory.push({ time: new Date(), bestProfitK: bestProfit, count: state.dumps.length });
    if (state.sniperHistory.length > 30) state.sniperHistory.shift();

    if (state.sniperHistory.length > 1) {
        updateChart('chartSniperSev', 'line', {
            labels: state.sniperHistory.map(h => h.time.toLocaleTimeString([],{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit',second:'2-digit'})),
            datasets: [
                { label:'Best Profit (K)', data:state.sniperHistory.map(h=>h.bestProfitK || h.maxCrash || h.severity || 0), borderColor:'#22c55e', backgroundColor:'rgba(34,197,94,0.1)', fill:true, tension:0.3, pointRadius:2 },
                { label:'Active Dumps', data:state.sniperHistory.map(h=>h.count), borderColor:'#ff981f', backgroundColor:'rgba(255,152,31,0.1)', fill:true, tension:0.3, pointRadius:2, yAxisID:'y2' },
            ]
        }, { plugins:{legend:{labels:{color:'#b8b0a5'}}}, scales:{ x:{ticks:{color:'#7a7268',maxTicksLimit:8},grid:{color:'rgba(255,152,31,0.08)'}}, y:{ticks:{color:'#ef4444'},grid:{color:'rgba(255,152,31,0.08)'}}, y2:{position:'right',ticks:{color:'#ff981f'},grid:{display:false}} }});
    }
}

function renderTopFlips(force = false) {
    let items = [...state.items];
    if (state.currentFilter) items = items.filter(i => i.name.toLowerCase().includes(state.currentFilter.toLowerCase()));
    if (state.verdictFilter !== 'all') {
        items = items.filter(i => {
            const verdict = getVerdict(i);
            return verdict.cls === state.verdictFilter;
        });
    }
    switch (state.currentSort) {
        case 'margin': items.sort((a,b) => b.margin - a.margin); break;
        case 'margin-pct': items.sort((a,b) => b.marginPct - a.marginPct); break;
        case 'volume': items.sort((a,b) => volPerHour(b) - volPerHour(a)); break;
        case 'price': items.sort((a,b) => b.sellPrice - a.sellPrice); break;
        default: items.sort((a,b) => realistic4hProfit(b) - realistic4hProfit(a));
    }

    // Skip re-render if data hasn't changed
    const hash = itemsHash(items);
    if (hash === state.lastRenderHash && !force) return;
    state.lastRenderHash = hash;

    const tbody = document.getElementById('topFlipsBody');
    if (tbody) {
        tbody.innerHTML = items.length > 0 ? items.map(item => {
            const v = getVerdict(item);
            const rp = realistic4hProfit(item);
            const rb = realisticBuys(item);
            const volumeLimited = item.buyLimit && (volPerHour(item) * 4) < item.buyLimit;
            const intel = MARKET_INTEL.getIntel(item);
            const intelToggleId = `intel-topflips-${item.itemId}`;
            const intelHtml = intel.length > 0 ? `
                <div style="margin-top:4px; display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">
                    <button class="intel-toggle" style="padding:0; margin:0;" onclick="document.getElementById('${intelToggleId}').classList.toggle('intel-hidden'); event.stopPropagation();">🧠</button>
                    <div id="${intelToggleId}" class="${state.showIntel ? '' : 'intel-hidden'}" style="display:${state.showIntel ? 'flex' : 'none'}; gap:4px; flex-wrap:wrap;">
                        ${intel.slice(0,2).map(i => `<span class="intel-badge ${i.tag}" title="${i.text.replace(/"/g,'&quot;')}" style="font-size:9px;">${i.icon} ${i.text.length > 40 ? i.text.slice(0,38)+'...' : i.text}</span>`).join('')}
                    </div>
                </div>
            ` : '';
            return `<tr onclick="openOSRSWiki('${item.name.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">
                <td onclick="event.stopPropagation(); toggleFav(${item.itemId},event.target.closest('button'))"><button class="fav-btn ${state.watchlist.has(item.itemId)?'on':''}" data-id="${item.itemId}" onclick="toggleFav(${item.itemId},this)">★</button></td>
                <td class="item-name-cell" style="max-width:300px;white-space:normal;"><span class="item-row-icon">${iconHtml(item.icon,item.name,32)}</span>${item.name}${intelHtml}</td>
                <td><span class="verdict-pill ${v.cls}" title="${v.tip}">${v.text}</span></td>
                <td style="font-size:16px; font-weight:800; color:var(--green);">${gp(item.buyPrice)}</td>
                <td style="font-size:16px; font-weight:800; color:var(--red);">${gp(item.sellPrice)}</td>
                <td class="price-gold" style="font-size:14px; font-weight:800;">${gp(item.margin)}</td>
                <td><span class="vol-context">${formatVolPerHour(item)}</span></td>
                <td class="price-hero">${gp(rp)}${volumeLimited ? '<br><span class="capped-warning">vol limited (~' + rb.toLocaleString() + ' avail)</span>' : ''}</td>
            </tr>`;
        }).join('') : '<tr><td colspan="8" class="empty-state">No items found</td></tr>';
    }

    const grid = document.getElementById('gridView');
    if (grid) {
        grid.innerHTML = items.map(item => {
            const v = getVerdict(item);
            const rp = realistic4hProfit(item);
            const intel = MARKET_INTEL.getIntel(item);
            const intelToggleId = `intel-card-${item.itemId}`;
            const topIntel = intel.length > 0 ? `
                <div style="margin-top:6px; text-align:center;">
                    <button class="intel-toggle" style="padding:0;" onclick="document.getElementById('${intelToggleId}').classList.toggle('intel-hidden'); event.stopPropagation();">🧠</button>
                    <div id="${intelToggleId}" class="${state.showIntel ? '' : 'intel-hidden'}" style="display:${state.showIntel ? 'flex' : 'none'}; gap:4px; flex-wrap:wrap; justify-content:center;">
                        <span class="intel-badge ${intel[0].tag}" title="${intel[0].text.replace(/"/g,'&quot;')}" style="font-size:9px;">${intel[0].icon} ${intel[0].text.length > 30 ? intel[0].text.slice(0,28)+'...' : intel[0].text}</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            ` : '';
            return `
            <div class="item-card" onclick="openOSRSWiki('${item.name.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">
                <button class="card-fav ${state.watchlist.has(item.itemId)?'on':''}" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); toggleFav(${item.itemId},this)">★</button>
                <div class="card-icon">${iconHtml(item.icon,item.name,48)}</div>
                <div class="card-name">${item.name}</div>
                <div class="card-jti"><span class="verdict-pill ${v.cls}">${v.text}</span></div>${topIntel}
                <div class="card-prices" style="grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;">
                    <div class="card-price-box"><div class="card-price-label">Buy</div><div class="price-green" style="font-size:16px;font-weight:800;">${gp(item.buyPrice)}</div></div>
                    <div class="card-price-box"><div class="card-price-label">Sell</div><div class="price-red" style="font-size:16px;font-weight:800;">${gp(item.sellPrice)}</div></div>
                </div>
                <div class="card-price-box" style="margin-bottom:6px;"><div class="card-price-label">Profit/Item</div><div class="price-gold" style="font-size:14px;font-weight:800;">${gp(item.margin)}</div></div>
                <div class="card-profit" style="background:rgba(34,197,94,0.15); color:var(--green); border:1px solid rgba(34,197,94,0.3); font-size:16px;">${gp(rp)}<br><span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-muted);font-weight:400;"> / 4h</span></div>
            </div>`;
        }).join('');
    }
}

function renderDumpsPumps() {
    // Skip re-render if dump/pump data hasn't changed
    const dumpsHash = state.dumps.map(d => `${d.itemId}:${d.flipProfit}`).join('|');
    if (dumpsHash === state.lastDumpsHash && state.pumps.length === 0) {
        // Still update charts
        renderSniperCharts(state.dumps);
        return;
    }
    state.lastDumpsHash = dumpsHash;

    const dc = document.getElementById('dumpsContainer'), pc = document.getElementById('pumpsContainer');
    if (dc) dc.innerHTML = state.dumps.length > 0 ? state.dumps.map(d => {
        const profit = d.flipProfit || (d.sellPrice - d.buyPrice - Math.min(Math.floor(d.sellPrice * 0.02), 5000000));
        return `
        <div class="dp-item" style="flex-wrap:wrap; gap:6px;">
            <div class="dp-item-icon">${iconHtml(d.icon,d.name,32)}</div>
            <div class="dp-item-name" style="min-width:100px;">${d.name}</div>
            <div style="display:flex; gap:6px; align-items:center; font-size:12px; margin-left:auto;">
                <span style="color:var(--green); font-weight:700;">Buy ${gp(d.instaBuyAt || d.buyPrice)}</span>
                <span style="color:var(--text-muted);">→</span>
                <span style="color:var(--accent); font-weight:700;">Sell ${gp(d.sellFor || d.sellPrice)}</span>
                <span style="color:var(--green); font-weight:800; font-size:13px; background:rgba(34,197,94,0.1); padding:2px 8px; border-radius:6px;">+${gp(profit)}</span>
            </div>
        </div>
    `}).join('') : '<div class="empty-state" style="padding:20px;"><p>No dumps detected — scanning every 8s</p></div>';
    if (pc) pc.innerHTML = state.pumps.length > 0 ? state.pumps.map(p => {
        return `
        <div class="dp-item">
            <div class="dp-item-icon">${iconHtml(p.icon,p.name,32)}</div>
            <div class="dp-item-name">${p.name}</div>
            <div style="display:flex; gap:6px; align-items:center; font-size:12px; margin-left:auto;">
                <span style="color:var(--green); font-weight:700;">${gp(p.buyPrice)}</span>
                <span style="color:var(--text-muted);">→</span>
                <span style="color:var(--accent); font-weight:700;">${gp(p.sellPrice)}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="dp-change pos" style="margin-left:10px; color:var(--green); font-weight:700;">${gp(p.sellPrice || 0)}</div>
        </div>
    `}).join('') : '<div class="empty-state" style="padding:20px;"><p>No pumps detected</p></div>';

    const allMovers = [...state.dumps, ...state.pumps].sort((a,b) => Math.abs(b.flipProfit || (b.sellPrice - b.buyPrice)) - Math.abs(a.flipProfit || (a.sellPrice - a.buyPrice))).slice(0, 12);
    if (allMovers.length > 0) {
        updateChart('chartMovers', 'bar', {
            labels: allMovers.map(m => m.name.length > 12 ? m.name.slice(0,11)+'...' : m.name),
            datasets: [{ data: allMovers.map(m => { const p = m.flipProfit || (m.sellPrice - m.buyPrice); return m.percentChange < 0 ? -Math.abs(p)/1000 : Math.abs(p)/1000; }), backgroundColor: allMovers.map(m => m.percentChange < 0 ? 'rgba(239,68,68,0.7)' : 'rgba(34,197,94,0.7)'), borderRadius:4 }]
        }, { indexAxis:'y', plugins:{legend:{display:false}}, scales:{ x:{ticks:{color:'#7a7268',callback:v=>gp(Math.abs(v*1000))},grid:{color:'rgba(255,152,31,0.08)'}}, y:{ticks:{color:'#b8b0a5',font:{size:11}},grid:{display:false}} }});
    }

    if (state.dpHistory.length > 1) {
        updateChart('chartDpHistory', 'line', {
            labels: state.dpHistory.map(h => h.time.toLocaleTimeString([],{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'})),
            datasets: [
                { label:'Dumps', data:state.dpHistory.map(h=>h.dumps), borderColor:'#ef4444', backgroundColor:'rgba(239,68,68,0.1)', fill:true, tension:0.3, pointRadius:2 },
                { label:'Pumps', data:state.dpHistory.map(h=>h.pumps), borderColor:'#22c55e', backgroundColor:'rgba(34,197,94,0.1)', fill:true, tension:0.3, pointRadius:2 },
            ]
        }, { plugins:{legend:{labels:{color:'#b8b0a5'}}}, scales:{ x:{ticks:{color:'#7a7268',maxTicksLimit:8},grid:{color:'rgba(255,152,31,0.08)'}}, y:{ticks:{color:'#7a7268'},grid:{color:'rgba(255,152,31,0.08)'}} }});
    }

    document.getElementById('statDumps').textContent = state.dumps.length;
    document.getElementById('statPumps').textContent = state.pumps.length;

    // Update badge
    const badge = document.getElementById('dumpsPumpsBadge');
    const totalDP = state.dumps.length + state.pumps.length;
    if (totalDP > 0) {
        badge.textContent = totalDP;
        badge.style.display = 'inline-block';
    } else {
        badge.style.display = 'none';
    }

    // Render Dump Sniper tab feed
    renderSniperFeed();
}

function renderWatchlist() {
    const watched = state.allItems.filter(i => state.watchlist.has(i.itemId));
    const content = document.getElementById('watchlistContent');
    const empty = document.getElementById('watchlistEmpty');

    // Update badge
    const badge = document.getElementById('watchlistBadge');
    if (watched.length > 0) {
        badge.textContent = watched.length;
        badge.style.display = 'inline-block';
    } else {
        badge.style.display = 'none';
    }

    if (watched.length > 0) {
        content.innerHTML = '<div class="item-grid">' + watched.map(item => {
            const v = getVerdict(item);
            const rp = realistic4hProfit(item);
            return `
            <div class="item-card" onclick="openOSRSWiki('${item.name.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">
                <button class="card-fav on" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); toggleFav(${item.itemId},this)">★</button>
                <div class="card-icon">${iconHtml(item.icon,item.name,48)}</div>
                <div class="card-name">${item.name}</div>
                <div class="card-jti"><span class="verdict-pill ${v.cls}">${v.text}</span></div>
                <div class="card-prices">
                    <div class="card-price-box"><div class="card-price-label">Buy</div><div class="price-green" style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;">${gp(item.buyPrice)}</div></div>
                    <div class="card-price-box"><div class="card-price-label">Sell</div><div class="price-red" style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;">${gp(item.sellPrice)}</div></div>
                </div>
                <div class="card-profit" style="background:rgba(34,197,94,0.1);color:var(--green);">${gp(rp)} / 4h<br><span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-muted);font-weight:400;">${gp(item.margin)}/item · ${formatVolPerHour(item)}</span></div>
            </div>`;
        }).join('') + '</div>';
        empty.classList.add('hidden');
    } else {
        content.innerHTML = '';
        empty.classList.remove('hidden');
    }
}

function renderRecipes() {
    const container = document.getElementById('recipesContainer');
    if (!container) return;
    let recipes = [...state.recipes];
    const sortBy = document.getElementById('recipeSort')?.value || 'profit';
    if (sortBy === 'roi') recipes.sort((a,b) => ((b.profit/b.inputPrice)||0) - ((a.profit/a.inputPrice)||0));
    else if (sortBy === 'name') recipes.sort((a,b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
    else recipes.sort((a,b) => b.profit - a.profit);
    const typeClass = t => t.includes('herb') ? 'herb' : t.includes('gem') ? 'gem' : t.includes('cook') ? 'cooking' : 'smelting';
    container.innerHTML = recipes.length > 0 ? recipes.map(r => `
        <div class="recipe-card">
            <div class="recipe-type-badge ${typeClass(r.type||'')}">${r.skill||r.type||''}</div>
            <div class="recipe-flow"><span class="r-in">${r.input}: ${gp(r.inputPrice)}</span><span class="r-arrow">→</span><span class="r-out">${r.output}: ${gp(r.outputPrice)}</span></div>
            <div class="recipe-profit-val">${gp(r.profit)}</div>
        </div>
    `).join('') : '<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-icon">🔬</div><p>No profitable recipes found</p></div>';
}
