// SPECIAL ITEMS
// ============================================
async function loadSpecialItems(cat) {
    const cid = { poisoned:'poisonedList', '3rd-age':'thirdAgeList', brutal:'brutalList', implings:'implingList' }[cat];
    const container = document.getElementById(cid);
    if (!container) return;
    container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state" style="padding:20px;"><p>Loading...</p></div>';
    let data = await fetchBackend(`/api/categories?type=${cat}`);
    if (!data) data = filterSpecial(cat);
    renderSpecial(cat, data, container);
}

function filterSpecial(cat) {
    const items = state.items;
    switch(cat) {
        case 'poisoned': return { poisoned: items.filter(i=>i.name&&(i.name.includes('(p)')||i.name.includes('(p+)')||i.name.includes('(p++)'))).map(i=>({name:i.name,icon:i.icon,buyPrice:i.buyPrice,sellPrice:i.sellPrice,profit:i.margin||0,tier:i.name.includes('(p++)')?'p++':i.name.includes('(p+)')?'p+':'p',volume:(i.buyQuantity||0)+(i.sellQuantity||0)}))};
        case '3rd-age': return { thirdAge: items.filter(i=>i.name&&i.name.toLowerCase().startsWith('3rd age')).map(i=>({name:i.name,icon:i.icon,buyPrice:i.buyPrice,sellPrice:i.sellPrice,margin:i.margin||0,geTax:Math.min(Math.floor((i.sellPrice||0)*0.02),5000000),volume:(i.buyQuantity||0)+(i.sellQuantity||0)}))};
        case 'brutal': return { brutal: items.filter(i=>i.name&&i.name.toLowerCase().includes('brutal')).map(i=>({name:i.name,icon:i.icon,buyPrice:i.buyPrice,sellPrice:i.sellPrice,flipMargin:i.margin||0,craftProfit:0,bestStrategy:'flip',volume:(i.buyQuantity||0)+(i.sellQuantity||0)}))};
        case 'implings': return { implings: items.filter(i=>i.name&&i.name.toLowerCase().includes('impling')).map(i=>({name:i.name,icon:i.icon,buyPrice:i.buyPrice,sellPrice:i.sellPrice,flipMargin:i.margin||0,expectedProfit:0,volume:(i.buyQuantity||0)+(i.sellQuantity||0)}))};
        default: return {};
    }
}

function renderSpecial(cat, data, container) {
    let items = [];
    switch(cat) {
        case 'poisoned': items = data.poisoned || []; break;
        case '3rd-age': items = data.thirdAge || []; break;
        case 'brutal': items = data.brutal || []; break;
        case 'implings': items = data.implings || []; break;
    }
    if (items.length === 0) { container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state" style="padding:20px;"><p>No items found. Data may still be loading.</p></div>'; return; }
    container.innerHTML = items.map(item => `
        <div class="dp-item" style="padding:10px 0; cursor:pointer;" onclick="openOSRSWiki('${item.name.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">
            <div class="dp-item-icon">${iconHtml(item.icon, item.name, 32)}</div>
            <div class="dp-item-name">${item.name}</div>
            <div style="display:flex;gap:12px;align-items:center;flex-shrink:0;">
                <span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">Buy: <span class="price-green">${gp(item.buyPrice)}</span></span>
                <span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">Sell: <span class="price-red">${gp(item.sellPrice)}</span></span>
                <span style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:${(item.profit||item.margin||item.flipMargin||0)>0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)'};">${gp(item.profit||item.margin||item.flipMargin||0)}</span>
            </div>
        </div>
    `).join('');
}

function toggleFav(id, btn) {
    if (state.watchlist.has(id)) state.watchlist.delete(id); else state.watchlist.add(id);
    if (btn) btn.classList.toggle('on');
    saveWatchlist();
    renderWatchlist();
}

        tab.classList.add('active');
        document.getElementById(tab.dataset.tab).classList.add('active');
    });
});

    state.currentFilter = e.target.value;
    // Auto-switch to Top Flips tab
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
    document.querySelectorAll('.tab-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
    const topFlipsTab = document.querySelector('[data-tab="top-flips"]');
    if (topFlipsTab) {
        topFlipsTab.classList.add('active');
        document.getElementById('top-flips').classList.add('active');
    }
    renderTopFlips();
});

document.getElementById('recipeSort')?.addEventListener('change', () => renderRecipes());

    }

async function init() {
    loadSettings();
    loadWatchlist();
    updateStatus(false);
    await loadTopFlips(true);
    updateStatus(state.allItems.length > 0);
    await loadDumpsPumps();
    await loadRecipes();
    loadSpecialItems('poisoned');
    startCountdownTimer();

    setInterval(async () => { try { await checkDumpsLight(); } catch {} }, state.dumpCheckInterval);

    async function smartRefresh() {
        try { await loadTopFlips(false); } catch {}
        state.refreshCountdown = Math.floor(state.fullRefreshInterval / 1000);
        setTimeout(smartRefresh, state.fullRefreshInterval);
    }
    setTimeout(smartRefresh, state.fullRefreshInterval);
}
window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
</script>

import discord
from discord.ext import commands, tasks
from discord import app_commands
import aiohttp
import os
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import json
import asyncio
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Tuple
import math

load_dotenv()

DISCORD_TOKEN = os.getenv('DISCORD_TOKEN')
API_URL = os.getenv('API_URL', 'http://localhost:3001')
WEBSITE_URL = os.getenv('WEBSITE_URL', 'https://tunatroll.github.io/grand-flip-out/')
BOT_INVITE_URL = 'https://discord.com/oauth2/authorize?client_id=1479089173209284608&permissions=1126745612873728&integration_type=0&scope=bot'
DUMP_ALERT_CHANNEL_ID = int(os.getenv('DUMP_ALERT_CHANNEL_ID', '0')) if os.getenv('DUMP_ALERT_CHANNEL_ID') else None
WATCHLIST_FILE = 'watchlists.json'

# OSRS Wiki API
WIKI_API_BASE = 'https://prices.runescape.wiki/api/v1/osrs'
WIKI_USER_AGENT = 'GrandFlipOut Discord Bot - OSRS flipping tool'

# OSRS colors
OSRS_GOLD = 0xFF981F
OSRS_GREEN = 0x00FF00
OSRS_RED = 0xFF0000
OSRS_BLUE = 0x0099FF

# Intents
intents = discord.Intents.default()
bot = commands.Bot(command_prefix='!', intents=intents)


class WikiApiClient:
    """Direct OSRS Wiki API client - works without backend server"""

    def __init__(self):
        self.session = None
        self.item_mapping = {}       # id -> {name, icon, limit, value, ...}
        self.item_by_name = {}       # lowercase name -> id
        self.latest_prices = {}      # id -> {high, low, highTime, lowTime}
        self.volume_data = {}        # id -> {buyVol, sellVol}
        self.prev_prices = {}        # id -> prev avg price (for dump detection)
        self.last_refresh = 0

    async def init_session(self):
        if self.session is None or self.session.closed:
            self.session = aiohttp.ClientSession(headers={'User-Agent': WIKI_USER_AGENT})

    async def close_session(self):
        if self.session and not self.session.closed:
            await self.session.close()

    async def wiki_get(self, endpoint: str) -> dict:
        """Fetch directly from OSRS Wiki API"""
        await self.init_session()
        try:
            url = f"{WIKI_API_BASE}{endpoint}"
            async with self.session.get(url, timeout=aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=15)) as resp:
                if resp.status == 200:
                    return await resp.json()
                else:
                    return {'error': f'Wiki API returned {resp.status}'}
        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
            return {'error': 'Wiki API timed out'}
        except Exception as e:
            return {'error': str(e)}

    async def load_mapping(self):
        """Load item ID -> name mapping from Wiki API"""
        data = await self.wiki_get('/mapping')
        if isinstance(data, list):
            self.item_mapping.clear()
            self.item_by_name.clear()
            for item in data:
                if not item or not item.get('id'):
                    continue
                item_id = item['id']
                self.item_mapping[item_id] = item
                name_lower = item.get('name', '').lower()
                if name_lower:
                    self.item_by_name[name_lower] = item_id
            print(f"Loaded {len(self.item_mapping)} items from Wiki mapping")
        else:
            print(f"Failed to load mapping: {data.get('error', 'unknown')}")

    async def refresh_prices(self):
        """Refresh latest prices and volumes from Wiki API"""
        latest = await self.wiki_get('/latest')
        volumes = await self.wiki_get('/5m')

        if 'data' in (latest or {}):
            for item_id, price_data in self.latest_prices.items():
                if price_data.get('high') and price_data.get('low'):
                    self.prev_prices[item_id] = (price_data['high'] + price_data['low']) // 2

            self.latest_prices = {}
            for id_str, price_data in latest['data'].items():
                if price_data and price_data.get('high') and price_data.get('low'):
                    self.latest_prices[int(id_str)] = price_data

        if 'data' in (volumes or {}):
            self.volume_data = {}
            for id_str, vol_data in volumes['data'].items():
                if vol_data:
                    self.volume_data[int(id_str)] = {
                        'buyVol': vol_data.get('lowPriceVolume', 0) or 0,
                        'sellVol': vol_data.get('highPriceVolume', 0) or 0,
                    }

        self.last_refresh = datetime.now().timestamp()
        print(f"Refreshed prices for {len(self.latest_prices)} items")

    def find_item_by_name(self, query: str) -> Optional[dict]:
        """Fuzzy match item by name"""
        if not self.item_mapping:
            return None

        query_lower = query.lower()

        # Exact match
        if query_lower in self.item_by_name:
            return self._build_item_data(self.item_by_name[query_lower])

        # Fuzzy match
        best_match_id = None
        best_ratio = 0
        for name_lower, item_id in self.item_by_name.items():
            ratio = SequenceMatcher(None, query_lower, name_lower).ratio()
            if ratio > best_ratio:
                best_ratio = ratio
                best_match_id = item_id

        if best_ratio > 0.6 and best_match_id:
            return self._build_item_data(best_match_id)
        return None

    def _build_item_data(self, item_id: int) -> dict:
        meta = self.item_mapping.get(item_id, {})
        prices = self.latest_prices.get(item_id, {})
        vols = self.volume_data.get(item_id, {})

        buy_price = prices.get('low', 0) or 0
        sell_price = prices.get('high', 0) or 0
        ge_tax = min(int(sell_price * 0.02), 5000000)
        margin = sell_price - buy_price - ge_tax

        return {
            'id': item_id,
            'name': meta.get('name', f'Item {item_id}'),
            'icon': meta.get('icon', ''),
            'buy_price': buy_price,
            'sell_price': sell_price,
            'current_price': (buy_price + sell_price) // 2 if buy_price and sell_price else 0,
            'margin': margin,
            'ge_tax': ge_tax,
            'jti': self._calculate_jti(item_id),
            'buy_volume': vols.get('buyVol', 0),
            'sell_volume': vols.get('sellVol', 0),
            'ge_limit': meta.get('limit', 0),
            'highalch': meta.get('highalch', 0),
        }

    def _calculate_jti(self, item_id: int) -> float:
        prices = self.latest_prices.get(item_id, {})
        vols = self.volume_data.get(item_id, {})

        buy_price = prices.get('low', 0) or 0
        sell_price = prices.get('high', 0) or 0
        high_time = prices.get('highTime', 0) or 0
        low_time = prices.get('lowTime', 0) or 0
        total_vol = (vols.get('buyVol', 0)) + (vols.get('sellVol', 0))

        # Freshness (15pts)
        freshness = 0
        if high_time or low_time:
            age = int(datetime.now().timestamp()) - max(high_time, low_time)
            if age < 30: freshness = 100
            elif age < 60: freshness = 95
            elif age < 120: freshness = 85
            elif age < 300: freshness = 70
            elif age < 600: freshness = 50
            elif age < 1200: freshness = 25
            else: freshness = max(0, 100 - (age / 600) * 100)

        # Liquidity (20pts)
        liquidity = 0
        if total_vol >= 100000: liquidity = 100
        elif total_vol >= 50000: liquidity = 90
        elif total_vol >= 10000: liquidity = 75
        elif total_vol >= 1000: liquidity = 50
        elif total_vol >= 100: liquidity = 25
        elif total_vol > 0: liquidity = min(100, (total_vol / 100) * 25)

        # Margin (20pts)
        margin_score = 0
        if buy_price > 0 and sell_price > 0:
            spread = (sell_price - buy_price) / buy_price
            if spread <= 0: margin_score = 0
            elif spread <= 0.025: margin_score = 40
            elif spread <= 0.05: margin_score = 100
            elif spread <= 0.10: margin_score = 80
            elif spread <= 0.20: margin_score = 50
            elif spread <= 0.40: margin_score = 25
            else: margin_score = max(0, 100 - spread * 50)

        # Velocity (15pts)
        velocity = 0
        if total_vol >= 10000: velocity = 100
        elif total_vol >= 5000: velocity = 90
        elif total_vol >= 1000: velocity = 75
        elif total_vol >= 500: velocity = 60
        elif total_vol >= 100: velocity = 45
        elif total_vol >= 50: velocity = 30
        elif total_vol >= 10: velocity = 15
        elif total_vol > 0: velocity = min(100, (total_vol / 10) * 15)

        jti = round((freshness * 15 + liquidity * 20 + margin_score * 20 + 50 * 15 + 50 * 15 + velocity * 15) / 100)
        return max(0, min(100, jti))

    def get_top_items(self, sort_by='realistic', limit=10):
        items = []
        for item_id in self.latest_prices:
            data = self._build_item_data(item_id)
            if data['margin'] > 0 and (data['buy_volume'] + data['sell_volume']) > 0:
                items.append(data)

        if sort_by == 'volume':
            items.sort(key=lambda x: x['buy_volume'] + x['sell_volume'], reverse=True)
        elif sort_by == 'margin':
            items.sort(key=lambda x: x.get('margin', 0), reverse=True)
        else:  # realistic (default)
            items.sort(key=lambda x: realistic_4h_profit(x), reverse=True)
        return items[:limit]

    # Junk items that should never trigger alerts
    JUNK_KEYWORDS = ['burnt ', 'broken ', 'damaged ', 'cake tin', 'pie dish', 'beer glass',
                     'wooden shield', 'leather body', 'leather chaps', 'bronze ', 'iron ',
                     'steel ', 'mithril ', 'adamant ', 'rune pickaxe', 'rune axe']

    def get_dumps(self, limit=10, for_alert=False):
        """Find items that crashed — with intelligent quality filtering.
        If for_alert=True, applies strict quality bars for auto-alerts."""
        dumps = []
        for item_id, prices in self.latest_prices.items():
            prev_avg = self.prev_prices.get(item_id)
            if not prev_avg or prev_avg == 0:
                continue

            meta = self.item_mapping.get(item_id, {})
            name = meta.get('name', f'Item {item_id}')
            name_lower = name.lower()

            # Skip junk items
            if any(junk in name_lower for junk in self.JUNK_KEYWORDS):
                continue

            # Normal value gate — use prev_avg as the "normal" price
            if prev_avg < 50000:
                continue

            current_buy = prices.get('low', 0) or 0
            current_sell = prices.get('high', 0) or 0
            if current_buy == 0 or current_sell == 0:
                continue

            # Volume gate
            vols = self.volume_data.get(item_id, {})
            total_vol = (vols.get('buyVol', 0)) + (vols.get('sellVol', 0))
            if total_vol < 3:
                continue

            # Calculate actual flip profit
            ge_tax = min(int(current_sell * 0.02), 5000000)
            flip_profit = current_sell - current_buy - ge_tax
            if flip_profit < 50000:
                continue

            # Estimate how many you can buy
            vol_per_hr = total_vol * 12
            vol_4h = vol_per_hr * 4
            ge_limit = meta.get('limit', 0) or 999999
            can_buy = min(ge_limit, int(vol_4h))
            total_profit = flip_profit * max(1, can_buy)

            # For auto-alerts: strict quality bar
            if for_alert:
                if flip_profit < 500000:
                    continue
                if current_buy < 500000:
                    continue
                if total_vol < 5:
                    continue
                if total_profit < 3000000:
                    continue

            dumps.append({
                'id': item_id,
                'name': name,
                'icon': meta.get('icon', ''),
                'buy_price': current_buy,
                'sell_price': current_sell,
                'flip_profit': flip_profit,
                'total_profit': total_profit,
                'can_buy': can_buy,
                'volume': total_vol,
                'normal_price': prev_avg,
            })

        # Sort by flip profit per item (best opportunities first)
        dumps.sort(key=lambda x: x['flip_profit'], reverse=True)
        return dumps[:limit]

    def get_pumps(self, limit=10):
        pumps = []
        for item_id in self.latest_prices:
            meta = self.item_mapping.get(item_id, {})
            name = meta.get('name', f'Item {item_id}')

            # Quality gate — skip junk
            if any(junk in name.lower() for junk in self.JUNK_KEYWORDS):
                continue

            prices = self.latest_prices.get(item_id, {})
            avg_price = ((prices.get('high', 0) or 0) + (prices.get('low', 0) or 0)) // 2
            if avg_price < 50000:
                continue

            vols = self.volume_data.get(item_id, {})
            bv, sv = vols.get('buyVol', 0), vols.get('sellVol', 0)
            if bv > sv * 1.5 and bv > 50:
                pumps.append({'name': name, 'buy_volume': bv, 'sell_volume': sv, 'avg_price': avg_price})
        pumps.sort(key=lambda x: x['buy_volume'], reverse=True)
        return pumps[:limit]

    def get_market_summary(self):
        total_volume = 0
        total_margin = 0
        count = 0
        top_item = None
        top_val = 0
        for item_id in self.latest_prices:
            d = self._build_item_data(item_id)
            v = d['buy_volume'] + d['sell_volume']
            total_volume += v
            if d['margin'] > 0:
                total_margin += d['margin']
                count += 1
                if d['margin'] > top_val:
                    top_val = d['margin']
                    top_item = d
        return {
            'total_volume': total_volume,
            'avg_margin': total_margin // max(1, count),
            'active_items': len(self.latest_prices),
            'top_item_by_margin': top_item,
        }


api_client = WikiApiClient()


def load_watchlists():
    if os.path.exists(WATCHLIST_FILE):
        try:
            with open(WATCHLIST_FILE, 'r') as f:
                return json.load(f)
        except:
            return {}
    return {}


def save_watchlists(watchlists):
    with open(WATCHLIST_FILE, 'w') as f:
        json.dump(watchlists, f, indent=2)


def format_gp(value):
    if value is None: return "N/A"
    if abs(value) >= 1000000: return f"{value/1000000:.1f}M gp"
    elif abs(value) >= 1000: return f"{value/1000:.1f}K gp"
    return f"{value:,} gp"

def vol_per_hour(item_data):
    """Estimate hourly volume from 5-min sample"""
    return (item_data.get('buy_volume', 0) + item_data.get('sell_volume', 0)) * 12

def realistic_buys(item_data):
    """How many you can actually buy in 4 hours = min(buy limit, 4h est. volume)"""
    vol_4h = vol_per_hour(item_data) * 4
    limit = item_data.get('ge_limit', 0) or 999999
    return min(limit, int(vol_4h))

def realistic_4h_profit(item_data):
    """Realistic 4-hour profit based on actual volume, not fantasy buy limits"""
    return item_data.get('margin', 0) * realistic_buys(item_data)

def get_verdict(item_data):
    """Human-readable flip quality based on margin AND volume"""
    vph = vol_per_hour(item_data)
    profit_4h = realistic_4h_profit(item_data)
    if vph < 12: return "Dead"
    if vph < 60 or profit_4h < 10000: return "Slow"
    if profit_4h < 100000 or vph < 200: return "Decent"
    if profit_4h < 500000: return "Good Flip"
    return "Great Flip"

def format_vol_per_hour(item_data):
    vph = vol_per_hour(item_data)
    if vph == 0: return "None"
    if vph < 12: return "<12/hr"
    if vph >= 10000: return f"{vph//1000}K/hr"
    if vph >= 1000: return f"{vph/1000:.1f}K/hr"
    return f"~{vph:,}/hr"

VERDICT_EMOJI = {
    "Great Flip": "🟢", "Good Flip": "🟡", "Decent": "🟠", "Slow": "🔴", "Dead": "⚫"
}


def get_item_icon_url(item_id, item_name="", icon=""):
    if icon:
        return f"https://oldschool.runescape.wiki/images/{icon.replace(' ', '_')}"
    if item_name:
        return f"https://oldschool.runescape.wiki/images/{item_name.replace(' ', '_')}.png"
    return f"https://oldschool.runescape.wiki/images/item_{item_id}.png"


async def create_item_embed(item_data, title=None):
    item_id = item_data.get('id')
    item_name = item_data.get('name', 'Unknown')
    verdict = get_verdict(item_data)
    emoji = VERDICT_EMOJI.get(verdict, "")
    embed = discord.Embed(title=title or f"{emoji} {item_name}", color=OSRS_GOLD)
    embed.set_thumbnail(url=get_item_icon_url(item_id, item_name, item_data.get('icon', '')))

    # Verdict
    embed.add_field(name="Verdict", value=f"**{verdict}**", inline=True)

    if item_data.get('buy_price'):
        embed.add_field(name="Buy Price", value=format_gp(item_data['buy_price']), inline=True)
    if item_data.get('sell_price'):
        embed.add_field(name="Sell Price", value=format_gp(item_data['sell_price']), inline=True)

    margin = item_data.get('margin', 0)
    embed.add_field(name="Profit/Item", value=f"{'+'if margin>0 else ''}{format_gp(margin)}", inline=True)
    if item_data.get('ge_tax'):
        embed.add_field(name="GE Tax", value=format_gp(item_data['ge_tax']), inline=True)

    # Volume info — honest
    embed.add_field(name="Volume", value=format_vol_per_hour(item_data), inline=True)

    # Realistic profit
    rp = realistic_4h_profit(item_data)
    rb = realistic_buys(item_data)
    ge_limit = item_data.get('ge_limit', 0)
    vol_limited = ge_limit and (vol_per_hour(item_data) * 4) < ge_limit
    profit_line = f"**{format_gp(rp)}** in 4 hours"
    if vol_limited:
        profit_line += f"\n⚠️ Vol limited: ~{rb:,} available (limit is {ge_limit:,})"
    embed.add_field(name="Realistic 4h Profit", value=profit_line, inline=False)

    embed.set_footer(text="Grand Flip Out | Real data, honest numbers")
    embed.timestamp = datetime.now()
    return embed


@bot.event
async def on_ready():
    print(f'{bot.user} has logged in')
    await api_client.load_mapping()
    await api_client.refresh_prices()
    refresh_prices_loop.start()
    check_dumps.start()
    try:
        synced = await bot.tree.sync()
        print(f"Synced {len(synced)} command(s)")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Failed to sync commands: {e}")
    print('Bot is ready!')


@tasks.loop(seconds=30)
async def refresh_prices_loop():
    await api_client.refresh_prices()

@refresh_prices_loop.before_loop
async def before_refresh():
    await bot.wait_until_ready()

@bot.tree.command(name="top", description="Show top items by realistic profit")
@app_commands.describe(sort="Sort by: realistic, margin, or volume", limit="Number of items (1-20)")
async def top_command(interaction: discord.Interaction, sort: str = "realistic", limit: int = 5):
    await interaction.response.defer()
    sort = sort.lower() if sort else "realistic"
    if sort not in ["realistic", "margin", "volume"]: sort = "realistic"
    limit = max(1, min(limit, 20))
    items = api_client.get_top_items(sort_by=sort, limit=limit)
    if not items:
        await interaction.followup.send("No items found. Data may still be loading.")
        return
    sort_label = {"realistic": "Realistic 4h Profit", "margin": "Profit per Item", "volume": "Volume"}[sort]
    embed = discord.Embed(title=f"Top {limit} Flips — {sort_label}", color=OSRS_GOLD, description="Ranked by what you can actually make, not fantasy numbers.")
    for i, item in enumerate(items, 1):
        n = item['name']
        verdict = get_verdict(item)
        emoji = VERDICT_EMOJI.get(verdict, "")
        rp = realistic_4h_profit(item)
        if sort == "realistic":
            v = f"{emoji} {verdict} | {format_gp(item['margin'])}/item → **{format_gp(rp)}/4h** | {format_vol_per_hour(item)}"
        elif sort == "margin":
            v = f"{emoji} {verdict} | **{format_gp(item['margin'])}**/item | {format_vol_per_hour(item)}"
        else:
            v = f"{emoji} {verdict} | **{format_vol_per_hour(item)}** | {format_gp(item['margin'])}/item"
        embed.add_field(name=f"{i}. {n}", value=v, inline=False)
    embed.set_footer(text="Grand Flip Out | Honest numbers from OSRS Wiki API")
    embed.timestamp = datetime.now()
    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed)

@bot.tree.command(name="recipe", description="Show profitable processing recipes")
async def recipe_command(interaction: discord.Interaction):
    await interaction.response.defer()
    herbs = [(249,251,'Guam'),(253,255,'Marrentill'),(257,259,'Tarromin'),(261,263,'Harralander'),(265,267,'Ranarr'),(269,271,'Irit'),(273,275,'Avantoe'),(277,279,'Kwuarm'),(281,283,'Cadantine'),(285,287,'Lantadyme'),(289,291,'Dwarf weed'),(293,295,'Torstol'),(301,303,'Snapdragon'),(305,307,'Toadflax')]
    gems = [(1617,1619,'Ruby'),(1621,1623,'Diamond'),(1625,1627,'Dragonstone'),(6573,6575,'Onyx')]
    profitable = []
    for raw_id, clean_id, name in herbs:
        rp = (api_client.latest_prices.get(raw_id, {}).get('low') or 0)
        cp = (api_client.latest_prices.get(clean_id, {}).get('high') or 0)
        if rp > 0 and cp > 0 and cp - rp > 0:
            profitable.append(('🌿', name, rp, cp, cp-rp, (cp-rp)*900))
    for raw_id, cut_id, name in gems:
        rp = (api_client.latest_prices.get(raw_id, {}).get('low') or 0)
        cp = (api_client.latest_prices.get(cut_id, {}).get('high') or 0)
        if rp > 0 and cp > 0 and cp - rp > 0:
            profitable.append(('💎', name, rp, cp, cp-rp, (cp-rp)*120))
    profitable.sort(key=lambda x: x[5], reverse=True)
    if not profitable:
        await interaction.followup.send("No profitable recipes at the moment.")
        return
    embed = discord.Embed(title="Profitable Processing Recipes", color=OSRS_BLUE, description="Herb cleaning (~900/hr) and gem cutting (~120/hr)")
    for i, (icon, name, buy, sell, profit, per_hr) in enumerate(profitable[:12], 1):
        embed.add_field(name=f"{i}. {icon} {name}", value=f"Buy: {format_gp(buy)} → Sell: {format_gp(sell)}\nProfit: {format_gp(profit)} | {format_gp(per_hr)}/hr", inline=False)
    embed.set_footer(text="Grand Flip Out | OSRS Wiki API")
    embed.timestamp = datetime.now()
    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed)


@bot.tree.command(name="analyze", description="Full flip analysis with realistic profit for an item")
@app_commands.describe(item_name="Name of the item")
async def analyze_command(interaction: discord.Interaction, item_name: str):
    await interaction.response.defer()
    item = api_client.find_item_by_name(item_name)
    if not item:
        await interaction.followup.send(f"Couldn't find item matching '{item_name}'.")
        return
    verdict = get_verdict(item)
    emoji = VERDICT_EMOJI.get(verdict, "")
    rp = realistic_4h_profit(item)
    rb = realistic_buys(item)
    vph = vol_per_hour(item)
    ge_limit = item.get('ge_limit', 0)
    vol_limited = ge_limit and (vph * 4) < ge_limit

    embed = discord.Embed(title=f"{emoji} {item['name']} — {verdict}", color=OSRS_GOLD)
    embed.set_thumbnail(url=get_item_icon_url(item['id'], item['name'], item.get('icon', '')))

    # Prices
    embed.add_field(name="Buy Price", value=format_gp(item['buy_price']), inline=True)
    embed.add_field(name="Sell Price", value=format_gp(item['sell_price']), inline=True)
    embed.add_field(name="Profit/Item", value=format_gp(item['margin']), inline=True)

    # Volume & limits
    embed.add_field(name="GE Tax", value=format_gp(item['ge_tax']), inline=True)
    embed.add_field(name="Volume", value=format_vol_per_hour(item), inline=True)
    embed.add_field(name="GE Limit", value=f"{ge_limit:,}" if ge_limit else "Unknown", inline=True)

    # The honest truth
    profit_text = f"**{format_gp(rp)}** in 4 hours"
    if vol_limited:
        profit_text += f"\n⚠️ Volume limited: only ~{rb:,} available per 4h"
        profit_text += f"\n(GE limit is {ge_limit:,} but not enough trades happening)"
    else:
        profit_text += f"\n~{rb:,} items tradeable in 4h"
    embed.add_field(name="Realistic Profit", value=profit_text, inline=False)

    # Quick verdict explanation
    if verdict == "Dead":
        embed.add_field(name="⚠️ Warning", value="Almost nobody is trading this item. Don't expect your offers to fill.", inline=False)
    elif verdict == "Slow":
        embed.add_field(name="💤 Note", value="Low activity. Your offers might take a while to fill.", inline=False)

    embed.set_footer(text="Grand Flip Out | Based on real trading volume")
    embed.timestamp = datetime.now()
    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed)

@bot.tree.command(name="compare", description="Compare two items side by side")
@app_commands.describe(item1="First item", item2="Second item")
async def compare_command(interaction: discord.Interaction, item1: str, item2: str):
    await interaction.response.defer()
    d1, d2 = api_client.find_item_by_name(item1), api_client.find_item_by_name(item2)
    if not d1 or not d2:
        await interaction.followup.send("Couldn't find one or both items.")
        return
    embed = discord.Embed(title=f"{d1['name']} vs {d2['name']}", color=OSRS_GOLD)
    embed.add_field(name="Buy Price", value=f"{d1['name']}: {format_gp(d1['buy_price'])}\n{d2['name']}: {format_gp(d2['buy_price'])}", inline=True)
    embed.add_field(name="Sell Price", value=f"{d1['name']}: {format_gp(d1['sell_price'])}\n{d2['name']}: {format_gp(d2['sell_price'])}", inline=True)
    embed.add_field(name="Net Profit", value=f"{d1['name']}: {format_gp(d1['margin'])}\n{d2['name']}: {format_gp(d2['margin'])}", inline=True)
    rp1, rp2 = realistic_4h_profit(d1), realistic_4h_profit(d2)
    v1, v2 = get_verdict(d1), get_verdict(d2)
    embed.add_field(name="Verdict", value=f"{d1['name']}: {VERDICT_EMOJI.get(v1,'')} {v1}\n{d2['name']}: {VERDICT_EMOJI.get(v2,'')} {v2}", inline=True)
    embed.add_field(name="4h Profit", value=f"{d1['name']}: {format_gp(rp1)}\n{d2['name']}: {format_gp(rp2)}", inline=True)
    winner = d1['name'] if rp1 > rp2 else d2['name']
    embed.add_field(name="Winner", value=f"**{winner}** makes more realistic profit", inline=False)
    embed.set_footer(text="Grand Flip Out | OSRS Wiki API")
    embed.timestamp = datetime.now()
    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed)


@bot.tree.command(name="watchlist", description="Manage your personal watchlist")
@app_commands.describe(action="add, remove, or show", item_name="Item name")
async def watchlist_command(interaction: discord.Interaction, action: str = "show", item_name: str = None):
    await interaction.response.defer()
    uid = str(interaction.user.id)
    wl = load_watchlists()
    if uid not in wl: wl[uid] = []
    action = action.lower()
    if action == "show":
        if not wl[uid]:
            await interaction.followup.send("Your watchlist is empty. Use `/watchlist add <item>` to add items!")
            return
        embed = discord.Embed(title=f"{interaction.user.name}'s Watchlist", color=OSRS_GOLD)
        for wn in wl[uid][:20]:
            item = api_client.find_item_by_name(wn)
            if item:
                v = get_verdict(item)
                rp = realistic_4h_profit(item)
                embed.add_field(name=f"{VERDICT_EMOJI.get(v,'')} {wn}", value=f"{format_gp(item['margin'])}/item | {format_gp(rp)}/4h | {format_vol_per_hour(item)}", inline=True)
        embed.set_footer(text="Grand Flip Out")
        await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed)
    elif action == "add":
        if not item_name:
            await interaction.followup.send("Specify an item name!")
            return
        item = api_client.find_item_by_name(item_name)
        if not item:
            await interaction.followup.send(f"Couldn't find '{item_name}'.")
            return
        n = item['name']
        if n not in wl[uid]:
            wl[uid].append(n)
            save_watchlists(wl)
            await interaction.followup.send(f"Added **{n}** to your watchlist!")
        else:
            await interaction.followup.send(f"**{n}** is already on your watchlist.")
    elif action == "remove":
        if not item_name:
            await interaction.followup.send("Specify an item name!")
            return
        item = api_client.find_item_by_name(item_name)
        if not item:
            await interaction.followup.send(f"Couldn't find '{item_name}'.")
            return
        n = item['name']
        if n in wl[uid]:
            wl[uid].remove(n)
            save_watchlists(wl)
            await interaction.followup.send(f"Removed **{n}** from your watchlist.")
        else:
            await interaction.followup.send(f"**{n}** is not on your watchlist.")
    else:
        await interaction.followup.send("Use 'add', 'remove', or 'show'.")


@bot.tree.command(name="sinks", description="Show items with high sell volume (GP sinks)")
async def sinks_command(interaction: discord.Interaction):
    await interaction.response.defer()
    sinks = []
    for item_id in api_client.latest_prices:
        vols = api_client.volume_data.get(item_id, {})
        bv, sv = vols.get('buyVol', 0), vols.get('sellVol', 0)
        if sv > bv * 1.5 and sv > 50:
            meta = api_client.item_mapping.get(item_id, {})
            sinks.append({'name': meta.get('name', f'Item {item_id}'), 'buy_volume': bv, 'sell_volume': sv})
    sinks.sort(key=lambda x: x['sell_volume'], reverse=True)
    if not sinks[:10]:
        await interaction.followup.send("No major GP sinks detected.")
        return
    embed = discord.Embed(title="GP Sinks", color=OSRS_RED)
    for item in sinks[:10]:
        embed.add_field(name=f"💸 {item['name']}", value=f"Buy: {item['buy_volume']:,} | Sell: {item['sell_volume']:,}", inline=False)
    embed.set_footer(text="Grand Flip Out | OSRS Wiki API")
    embed.timestamp = datetime.now()
    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed)

# Rate limiting state for auto-alerts
_alert_last_global = 0          # timestamp of last alert sent
_alert_item_times = {}          # item_id -> last alert timestamp
_alert_count_this_hour = []     # list of timestamps for alerts sent this hour
ALERT_GLOBAL_COOLDOWN = 900     # 15 minutes between any alerts
ALERT_ITEM_COOLDOWN = 3600      # 1 hour before same item can alert again
ALERT_MAX_PER_HOUR = 4          # max 4 alerts per hour total


@tasks.loop(minutes=5)
async def check_dumps():
    """Post only the best dump opportunities. Clean format: just buy, sell, profit."""
    global _alert_last_global, _alert_item_times, _alert_count_this_hour
    if not DUMP_ALERT_CHANNEL_ID:
        return
    try:
        ch = bot.get_channel(DUMP_ALERT_CHANNEL_ID)
        if not ch:
            return

        now = datetime.now().timestamp()

        # Global cooldown
        if now - _alert_last_global < ALERT_GLOBAL_COOLDOWN:
            return

        # Prune hourly counter
        _alert_count_this_hour = [t for t in _alert_count_this_hour if now - t < 3600]
        if len(_alert_count_this_hour) >= ALERT_MAX_PER_HOUR:
            return

        # Get dumps with strict quality filtering
        dumps = api_client.get_dumps(limit=3, for_alert=True)
        if not dumps:
            return

        sent = 0
        for d in dumps:
            if sent >= 1:
                break  # Only send 1 alert per cycle max

            item_id = d.get('id', 0)

            # Per-item cooldown
            if item_id in _alert_item_times and now - _alert_item_times[item_id] < ALERT_ITEM_COOLDOWN:
                continue

            # Build the clean embed — JUST THE MONEY
            embed = discord.Embed(
                title=f"💰 {d['name']} — {format_gp(d['flip_profit'])}/item",
                description=f"Buy **{format_gp(d['buy_price'])}** → Sell **{format_gp(d['sell_price'])}** → **{format_gp(d['total_profit'])}** total",
                color=0x22C55E,
            )
            icon = d.get('icon', '')
            if icon:
                embed.set_thumbnail(url=f"https://oldschool.runescape.wiki/images/{icon.replace(' ', '_')}")
            embed.set_footer(text="Grand Flip Out")
            embed.timestamp = datetime.now()

            await ch.send(embed=embed)

            # Update rate limits
            _alert_last_global = now
            _alert_item_times[item_id] = now
            _alert_count_this_hour.append(now)
            sent += 1

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Dump check error: {e}")

@check_dumps.before_loop
async def before_check_dumps():
    await bot.wait_until_ready()


async def main():
    async with bot:
        await bot.start(DISCORD_TOKEN)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        asyncio.run(main())
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("Bot shutting down...")
    finally:
        try:
            asyncio.run(api_client.close_session())
        except:
            pass

# Discord Bot Token — paste your token on the line below
DISCORD_TOKEN=REDACTED_DISCORD_TOKEN

# API Configuration — points to your backend server
API_URL=http://localhost:3001

# Public website URL (shared in /website and /invite commands)
WEBSITE_URL=https://tunatroll.github.io/grand-flip-out/

# Channel ID for automatic dump alerts
DUMP_ALERT_CHANNEL_ID=1479280773029957705



============================================================
FILE: SERVER — index.js
PATH: server/index.js
============================================================

#!/usr/bin/env node

/**
 * Grand Flip Out - OSRS Grand Exchange Flipping Tool
 * Backend API Server
 *
 * Main entry point: starts Express server with WebSocket support,
 * initializes API scanner, and manages real-time price updates.
 */

import 'dotenv/config.js';
import express from 'express';
import cors from 'cors';
import { WebSocketServer } from 'ws';
import http from 'http';
import path from 'path';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'url';
import APIScanner from './scanner.js';
import JTICalculator from './jti.js';
import RecipeCalculator from './recipes.js';
import routes, { initializeRoutes } from './routes.js';

// Configuration
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3001;
const NODE_ENV = process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development';

// Initialize core components
const scanner = new APIScanner();
const jtiCalculator = new JTICalculator();
const recipeCalculator = new RecipeCalculator();

// Create Express app
const app = express();

// Middleware
app.use(cors({
  origin: '*',
  methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'OPTIONS'],
  credentials: false
}));
app.use(express.json());

// Serve the website from ../website
const __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
const __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
app.use(express.static(path.join(__dirname, '..', 'website')));

// Initialize routes
initializeRoutes(scanner, jtiCalculator, recipeCalculator, null);
app.use('/api', routes);

// Health check endpoint
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.json({ status: 'ok', timestamp: Date.now() });
});

// Serve website for any non-API route
app.get('*', (req, res) => {
  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, '..', 'website', 'index.html'));
});

// Error handler
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  console.error('Error:', err);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error' });
});

// Create HTTP server for WebSocket support
const server = http.createServer(app);

// WebSocket server configuration
const wss = new WebSocketServer({ server });
const clients = new Set();

/**
 * Broadcast message to all connected WebSocket clients
 */
function broadcastToClients(data) {
  const message = JSON.stringify(data);
  clients.forEach(client => {
    if (client.readyState === 1) { // OPEN
      client.send(message, err => {
        if (err && err.code !== 1000) {
          console.error('WebSocket send error:', err.message);
        }
      });
    }
  });
}

// WebSocket connection handler
wss.on('connection', (ws) => {
  console.log(`WebSocket client connected. Total: ${clients.size + 1}`);
  clients.add(ws);

  // Send initial status
  ws.send(JSON.stringify({
    type: 'connected',
    message: 'Connected to Grand Flip Out server',
    timestamp: Date.now()
  }));

  ws.on('message', (data) => {
    try {
      const message = JSON.parse(data);
      console.log('WebSocket message:', message.type);

      // Handle different message types
      switch (message.type) {
        case 'ping':
          ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'pong', timestamp: Date.now() }));
          break;
        case 'subscribe':
          // Client can subscribe to specific items or all updates
          ws.itemSubscriptions = new Set(message.items || []);
          ws.send(JSON.stringify({
            type: 'subscribed',
            items: Array.from(ws.itemSubscriptions),
            timestamp: Date.now()
          }));
          break;
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('WebSocket message error:', error.message);
    }
  });

  ws.on('close', () => {
    clients.delete(ws);
    console.log(`WebSocket client disconnected. Total: ${clients.size}`);
  });

  ws.on('error', (error) => {
    console.error('WebSocket error:', error.message);
    clients.delete(ws);
  });
});

/**
 * Update recipe calculator with live price data from scanner
 */
function updateRecipeData() {
  const priceMap = {};
  scanner.itemPrices.forEach((priceData, itemId) => {
    priceMap[itemId] = priceData;
  });
  recipeCalculator.updateItemData(priceMap);
}

/**
 * Push price updates to connected clients
 * Runs after each /latest scan
 */
function pushPriceUpdates() {
  const items = scanner.getAllItems()
    .filter(item => item !== null)
    .slice(0, 50) // Send top 50 items for performance
    .map(item => {
      const history = scanner.getHistory(item.itemId, 5);
      const jtiScore = jtiCalculator.calculateJTI(item, history);
      return {
        itemId: item.itemId,
        name: item.mapping?.name || `Item ${item.itemId}`,
        prices: {
          buy: item.lowPrice,
          sell: item.highPrice,
          avg: item.avg
        },
        jti: jtiScore.jti,
        volume: item.buyQuantity + item.sellQuantity,
        timestamp: item.timestamp
      };
    });

  broadcastToClients({
    type: 'price_update',
    items,
    timestamp: Date.now()
  });
}

/**
 * Push dump alerts to clients
 */
function pushDumpAlerts() {
  const dumps = scanner.getDumpAlerts(10);
  if (dumps.length > 0) {
    broadcastToClients({
      type: 'dump_alert',
      dumps,
      timestamp: Date.now()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Monitor for new dumps and push alerts
 */
let lastDumpCount = 0;
setInterval(() => {
  const currentDumpCount = scanner.getDumpAlerts().length;
  if (currentDumpCount > lastDumpCount) {
    pushDumpAlerts();
    lastDumpCount = currentDumpCount;
  }
}, 5000);

/**
 * Push price updates every 15 seconds (aligned with scanner updates)
 * Also refresh recipe calculator data
 */
setInterval(() => {
  updateRecipeData();
  if (clients.size > 0) {
    pushPriceUpdates();
  }
}, 15000);

// Start the scanner and server
async function start() {
  try {
    // Start API scanner
    await scanner.start();

    // Start HTTP/WebSocket server
    server.listen(PORT, () => {
      console.log(`
╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║         Grand Flip Out - OSRS GE Flipping Tool              ║
║                    Backend API Server                        ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

Server running on port ${PORT}
Environment: ${NODE_ENV}

Endpoints:
  REST API: http://localhost:${PORT}/api
  WebSocket: ws://localhost:${PORT}
  Health: http://localhost:${PORT}/health

Scanner Status:
  /latest polling: 15 seconds
  /5m polling: 60 seconds
  Mapping refresh: 1 hour

Available Routes:
  GET  /api/items - All items with prices and JTI
  GET  /api/items/:id - Single item details
  GET  /api/items/:id/history - Price history
  GET  /api/dumps - Current dumps and spikes
  GET  /api/top - Top 10 by metric
  GET  /api/recipes - Recipe profit calculator
  GET  /api/market - Market overview
  GET  /api/status - Server health and stats
  WS   /ws - Real-time price and dump alerts

Press Ctrl+C to stop
      `);
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to start server:', error);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

// Handle graceful shutdown
process.on('SIGINT', () => {
  console.log('\nShutting down server...');
  scanner.stop();
  wss.close();
  server.close(() => {
    console.log('Server closed');
    process.exit(0);
  });
});

process.on('SIGTERM', () => {
  console.log('\nShutting down server...');
  scanner.stop();
  wss.close();
  server.close(() => {
    console.log('Server closed');
    process.exit(0);
  });
});

// Start the server
start();



============================================================
FILE: SERVER — jti.js
PATH: server/jti.js
============================================================

/**
 * JTI (Jump Trade Index) Scoring Algorithm
 *
 * A comprehensive scoring system (0-100) for OSRS Grand Exchange items
 * based on multiple trading indicators.
 *
 * Scoring breakdown:
 * - Freshness (15pts): Recent trade activity
 * - Liquidity (20pts): Trade volume
 * - Margin (20pts): Buy/sell spread
 * - Momentum (15pts): Price direction
 * - Stability (15pts): Spread consistency
 * - Velocity (15pts): Trade frequency
 */

export class JTICalculator {
  constructor() {
    // Configuration for score weights and thresholds
    this.config = {
      freshness: { weight: 15, maxAgeSeconds: 600 },
      liquidity: { weight: 20, volumeThreshold: 100 },
      margin: { weight: 20, targetSpread: 0.05 },
      momentum: { weight: 15 },
      stability: { weight: 15 },
      velocity: { weight: 15, tradeWindow: 300 }
    };
  }

  /**
   * Calculate complete JTI score for an item
   * @param {Object} itemData - Current item data with price/volume info
   * @param {Array} priceHistory - Historical price data points
   * @returns {Object} Score breakdown and total JTI
   */
  calculateJTI(itemData, priceHistory = []) {
    const scores = {
      freshness: this.calculateFreshness(itemData),
      liquidity: this.calculateLiquidity(itemData),
      margin: this.calculateMargin(itemData),
      momentum: this.calculateMomentum(itemData, priceHistory),
      stability: this.calculateStability(itemData, priceHistory),
      velocity: this.calculateVelocity(itemData)
    };

    // Calculate weighted total
    const totalJTI = Math.round(
      (scores.freshness * this.config.freshness.weight +
       scores.liquidity * this.config.liquidity.weight +
       scores.margin * this.config.margin.weight +
       scores.momentum * this.config.momentum.weight +
       scores.stability * this.config.stability.weight +
       scores.velocity * this.config.velocity.weight) / 100
    );

    return {
      jti: Math.max(0, Math.min(100, totalJTI)),
      breakdown: scores,
      weights: {
        freshness: this.config.freshness.weight,
        liquidity: this.config.liquidity.weight,
        margin: this.config.margin.weight,
        momentum: this.config.momentum.weight,
        stability: this.config.stability.weight,
        velocity: this.config.velocity.weight
      }
    };
  }

  /**
   * Freshness Score (0-100)
   * How recently the item was traded
   */
  calculateFreshness(itemData) {
    if (!itemData.highTime && !itemData.lowTime) {
      return 0;
    }

    const latestTime = Math.max(itemData.highTime || 0, itemData.lowTime || 0);
    const ageSeconds = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) - latestTime;
    const maxAge = this.config.freshness.maxAgeSeconds;

    if (ageSeconds < 30) return 100; // Very fresh
    if (ageSeconds < 60) return 95;
    if (ageSeconds < 120) return 85;
    if (ageSeconds < 300) return 70;
    if (ageSeconds < 600) return 50;
    if (ageSeconds < 1200) return 25;
    return Math.max(0, 100 - (ageSeconds / maxAge) * 100);
  }

  /**
   * Liquidity Score (0-100)
   * Based on buy/sell volume
   */
  calculateLiquidity(itemData) {
    const buyVolume = itemData.buyQuantity || 0;
    const sellVolume = itemData.sellQuantity || 0;
    const totalVolume = buyVolume + sellVolume;
    const threshold = this.config.liquidity.volumeThreshold;

    if (totalVolume === 0) return 0;
    if (totalVolume >= threshold * 1000) return 100; // Excellent liquidity
    if (totalVolume >= threshold * 500) return 90;
    if (totalVolume >= threshold * 100) return 75;
    if (totalVolume >= threshold * 10) return 50;
    if (totalVolume >= threshold) return 25;
    return Math.min(100, (totalVolume / threshold) * 25);
  }

  /**
   * Margin Score (0-100)
   * Based on buy/sell spread
   * Higher spread = better margin but lower liquidity
   */
  calculateMargin(itemData) {
    const buyPrice = itemData.highPrice || 0;
    const sellPrice = itemData.lowPrice || 0;

    if (buyPrice === 0 || sellPrice === 0) {
      return 0;
    }

    const spread = (buyPrice - sellPrice) / sellPrice;
    const targetSpread = this.config.margin.targetSpread;

    // Score peaks at target spread, penalizes both low and high spreads
    if (spread < 0) return 0; // Invalid spread

    if (spread === 0) return 20; // No spread
    if (spread <= targetSpread / 2) return 40;
    if (spread <= targetSpread) return 100; // Ideal margin
    if (spread <= targetSpread * 2) return 80;
    if (spread <= targetSpread * 4) return 50;
    if (spread <= targetSpread * 8) return 25;
    return Math.max(0, 100 - spread * 50); // Heavily penalize extreme spreads
  }

  /**
   * Momentum Score (0-100)
   * Based on price trend direction and magnitude
   */
  calculateMomentum(itemData, priceHistory = []) {
    if (priceHistory.length < 2) {
      return 50; // Neutral if no history
    }

    // Use last 10 data points or available history
    const recentHistory = priceHistory.slice(-10);
    const currentPrice = (itemData.highPrice + itemData.lowPrice) / 2;
    const previousPrice = recentHistory[recentHistory.length - 2].avg || currentPrice;

    const priceChange = ((currentPrice - previousPrice) / previousPrice) * 100;

    if (priceChange > 5) return 100; // Strong uptrend
    if (priceChange > 2) return 85;
    if (priceChange > 0) return 70;
    if (priceChange === 0) return 50; // Neutral
    if (priceChange > -2) return 35;
    if (priceChange > -5) return 20;
    return Math.max(0, 100 + priceChange * 5); // Downtrend
  }

  /**
   * Stability Score (0-100)
   * Based on consistency of spread over time
   */
  calculateStability(itemData, priceHistory = []) {
    if (priceHistory.length < 3) {
      return 50; // Neutral if insufficient history
    }

    // Calculate spread variance over recent history
    const recentHistory = priceHistory.slice(-10);
    const spreads = recentHistory.map(point => {
      const price = point.avg || point.price || 0;
      const spread = (point.highPrice - point.lowPrice) / price || 0;
      return spread;
    });

    const avgSpread = spreads.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / spreads.length;
    const variance = spreads.reduce((sum, spread) => sum + Math.pow(spread - avgSpread, 2), 0) / spreads.length;
    const stdDev = Math.sqrt(variance);

    // Lower std dev = higher stability
    if (stdDev < 0.002) return 100;
    if (stdDev < 0.005) return 90;
    if (stdDev < 0.01) return 75;
    if (stdDev < 0.02) return 50;
    if (stdDev < 0.05) return 25;
    return Math.max(0, 100 - stdDev * 1000);
  }

  /**
   * Velocity Score (0-100)
   * Based on trade frequency and activity
   */
  calculateVelocity(itemData) {
    const buyVolume = itemData.buyQuantity || 0;
    const sellVolume = itemData.sellQuantity || 0;
    const totalVolume = buyVolume + sellVolume;

    // Volume per time unit indicator
    if (totalVolume === 0) return 0;
    if (totalVolume >= 10000) return 100; // Very active
    if (totalVolume >= 5000) return 90;
    if (totalVolume >= 1000) return 75;
    if (totalVolume >= 500) return 60;
    if (totalVolume >= 100) return 45;
    if (totalVolume >= 50) return 30;
    if (totalVolume >= 10) return 15;
    return Math.min(100, (totalVolume / 10) * 15);
  }

  /**
   * Detect sudden price dumps (>5% in 5min window)
   * @param {Array} priceHistory - Recent price data
   * @returns {Boolean} True if dump detected
   */
  detectDump(priceHistory = []) {
    if (priceHistory.length < 2) return false;

    const recent = priceHistory.slice(-12); // ~5min at 25s intervals
    if (recent.length < 2) return false;

    const current = recent[recent.length - 1].avg || recent[recent.length - 1].price;
    const previous = recent[0].avg || recent[0].price;

    const priceChange = ((current - previous) / previous) * 100;
    return priceChange < -5; // More than 5% drop
  }

  /**
   * Detect volume spikes (2x average volume)
   * @param {Object} itemData - Current item data
   * @param {Array} volumeHistory - Historical volume data
   * @returns {Boolean} True if spike detected
   */
  detectVolumeSpike(itemData, volumeHistory = []) {
    if (volumeHistory.length < 5) return false;

    const currentVolume = (itemData.buyQuantity || 0) + (itemData.sellQuantity || 0);
    const avgVolume = volumeHistory
      .slice(-20)
      .reduce((sum, v) => sum + v, 0) / Math.min(20, volumeHistory.length);

    return currentVolume > avgVolume * 2 && avgVolume > 0;
  }
}

export default JTICalculator;



============================================================
FILE: SERVER — categories.js
PATH: server/categories.js
============================================================

/**
 * Item Category Engine
 * Classifies OSRS items into flipping-relevant categories
 * and provides category-specific intelligence.
 */

export class ItemCategoryEngine {
  constructor() {
    this.categoryCache = new Map();
    this.initPatterns();
  }

  initPatterns() {
    // ========================================
    // POISONED ITEMS
    // ========================================
    this.poisonedPatterns = {
      // Weapon poison variants: (p), (p+), (p++)
      suffixes: ['(p)', '(p+)', '(p++)'],
      // Known poisoned weapon bases
      bases: [
        'dagger', 'spear', 'hasta', 'javelin', 'knife',
        'arrow', 'bolt', 'dart'
      ],
      // Specific named items
      specific: [
        'Emerald bolts (e)', 'Dragon bolts (e)'
      ]
    };

    // ========================================
    // 3RD AGE ITEMS
    // ========================================
    this.thirdAgePatterns = {
      prefixes: ['3rd age'],
      // Full list of 3rd age item types
      types: [
        'platebody', 'platelegs', 'plateskirt', 'full helmet', 'kiteshield',
        'range top', 'range legs', 'range coif', 'vambraces',
        'robe top', 'robe', 'mage hat', 'amulet',
        'cloak', 'longsword', 'bow', 'wand',
        'druidic robe top', 'druidic robe bottoms', 'druidic staff', 'druidic cloak',
        'pickaxe', 'axe'
      ]
    };

    // ========================================
    // BRUTAL ARROWS
    // ========================================
    this.brutalPatterns = {
      names: [
        'Bronze brutal', 'Iron brutal', 'Steel brutal',
        'Black brutal', 'Mithril brutal', 'Adamant brutal',
        'Rune brutal'
      ]
    };

    // ========================================
    // IMPLINGS
    // ========================================
    this.implingPatterns = {
      // Impling jars (the tradeable items)
      jarSuffix: 'impling jar',
      types: [
        'Baby', 'Young', 'Gourmet', 'Earth', 'Essence',
        'Eclectic', 'Nature', 'Magpie', 'Ninja',
        'Crystal', 'Dragon', 'Lucky'
      ],
      // Expected value data for impling jars (approximate avg loot value in GP)
      expectedValues: {
        'Baby impling jar': 2500,
        'Young impling jar': 5000,
        'Gourmet impling jar': 7500,
        'Earth impling jar': 12000,
        'Essence impling jar': 15000,
        'Eclectic impling jar': 22000,
        'Nature impling jar': 45000,
        'Magpie impling jar': 75000,
        'Ninja impling jar': 120000,
        'Crystal impling jar': 280000,
        'Dragon impling jar': 550000,
        'Lucky impling jar': 750000
      }
    };
  }

  /**
   * Classify an item into categories
   * Returns an object with all applicable categories and metadata
   */
  classify(itemName) {
    if (!itemName) return { categories: [], tags: [] };

    // Check cache
    if (this.categoryCache.has(itemName)) {
      return this.categoryCache.get(itemName);
    }

    const result = {
      categories: [],
      tags: [],
      meta: {}
    };

    const nameLower = itemName.toLowerCase();

    // Check poisoned
    const poisonInfo = this.checkPoisoned(itemName, nameLower);
    if (poisonInfo) {
      result.categories.push('poisoned');
      result.tags.push(poisonInfo.tier);
      result.meta.poison = poisonInfo;
    }

    // Check 3rd age
    if (this.checkThirdAge(nameLower)) {
      result.categories.push('3rd-age');
      result.tags.push('rare');
      result.meta.thirdAge = { rarity: 'extremely-rare', source: 'treasure-trails' };
    }

    // Check brutal
    if (this.checkBrutal(nameLower)) {
      result.categories.push('brutal');
      result.tags.push('ammo');
      result.meta.brutal = { type: 'arrow', combatStyle: 'ranged' };
    }

    // Check impling
    const implingInfo = this.checkImpling(itemName, nameLower);
    if (implingInfo) {
      result.categories.push('impling');
      result.tags.push(implingInfo.tier);
      result.meta.impling = implingInfo;
    }

    // Additional useful categories
    if (nameLower.includes('(noted)')) result.tags.push('noted');
    if (nameLower.includes('(unf)')) { result.categories.push('unfinished-potion'); result.tags.push('potion'); }
    if (nameLower.match(/\(\d\)$/)) { result.categories.push('dose-potion'); result.tags.push('potion'); }
    if (nameLower.includes('grimy')) { result.categories.push('grimy-herb'); result.tags.push('herb'); }

    this.categoryCache.set(itemName, result);
    return result;
  }

  checkPoisoned(name, nameLower) {
    // Check for (p), (p+), (p++) suffixes
    if (name.includes('(p++)')) {
      return { tier: 'p++', poisonDamage: 6, baseName: name.replace('(p++)', '').trim() };
    }
    if (name.includes('(p+)')) {
      return { tier: 'p+', poisonDamage: 4, baseName: name.replace('(p+)', '').trim() };
    }
    if (name.match(/\(p\)$/)) {
      return { tier: 'p', poisonDamage: 2, baseName: name.replace('(p)', '').trim() };
    }
    return null;
  }

  checkThirdAge(nameLower) {
    return nameLower.startsWith('3rd age');
  }

  checkBrutal(nameLower) {
    return nameLower.includes('brutal') && (
      nameLower.includes('bronze brutal') ||
      nameLower.includes('iron brutal') ||
      nameLower.includes('steel brutal') ||
      nameLower.includes('black brutal') ||
      nameLower.includes('mithril brutal') ||
      nameLower.includes('adamant brutal') ||
      nameLower.includes('rune brutal')
    );
  }

  checkImpling(name, nameLower) {
    if (!nameLower.includes('impling')) return null;

    const isJar = nameLower.includes('jar');
    let tier = 'common';
    let type = 'unknown';

    for (const t of this.implingPatterns.types) {
      if (nameLower.includes(t.toLowerCase())) {
        type = t;
        break;
      }
    }

    // Determine tier
    const highTier = ['Dragon', 'Lucky', 'Crystal'];
    const midTier = ['Ninja', 'Magpie', 'Nature'];
    const lowTier = ['Eclectic', 'Essence', 'Earth', 'Gourmet'];

    if (highTier.includes(type)) tier = 'high-value';
    else if (midTier.includes(type)) tier = 'mid-value';
    else if (lowTier.includes(type)) tier = 'low-value';
    else tier = 'common';

    const expectedValue = this.implingPatterns.expectedValues[name] || 0;

    return {
      type,
      isJar,
      tier,
      expectedValue,
      source: isJar ? 'puro-puro' : 'world-spawn'
    };
  }

  /**
   * Get poisoned item profit analysis
   * Compares base weapon price vs poisoned variant prices
   */
  analyzePoisonedProfit(allItems) {
    const poisonedItems = [];
    const baseItems = new Map();

    // First pass — find all poisoned items and their bases
    for (const item of allItems) {
      if (!item || !item.name) continue;
      const cat = this.classify(item.name);

      if (cat.categories.includes('poisoned')) {
        poisonedItems.push({ ...item, poisonMeta: cat.meta.poison });
      } else {
        // Index by name for lookup
        baseItems.set(item.name.toLowerCase(), item);
      }
    }

    // Second pass — calculate profit from poisoning
    return poisonedItems.map(pItem => {
      const baseName = pItem.poisonMeta.baseName.toLowerCase();
      const baseItem = baseItems.get(baseName);

      const poisonCost = this.getPoisonCost(pItem.poisonMeta.tier);
      const basePrice = baseItem ? (baseItem.buyPrice || baseItem.lowPrice || 0) : 0;
      const poisonedPrice = pItem.sellPrice || pItem.highPrice || 0;
      const profit = poisonedPrice - basePrice - poisonCost;

      return {
        name: pItem.name,
        itemId: pItem.itemId,
        icon: pItem.icon || pItem.mapping?.icon,
        tier: pItem.poisonMeta.tier,
        basePrice,
        poisonedPrice,
        poisonCost,
        profit,
        baseName: pItem.poisonMeta.baseName,
        baseItemId: baseItem?.itemId || null,
        jti: pItem.jti || pItem.jtiScore || 0,
        volume: (pItem.buyQuantity || 0) + (pItem.sellQuantity || 0)
      };
    }).filter(i => i.profit !== 0).sort((a, b) => b.profit - a.profit);
  }

  getPoisonCost(tier) {
    // Approximate weapon poison costs
    switch (tier) {
      case 'p': return 200;     // Weapon poison
      case 'p+': return 2500;   // Weapon poison(+)
      case 'p++': return 7500;  // Weapon poison(++)
      default: return 0;
    }
  }

  /**
   * Analyze impling jar expected profits
   * Compares jar cost vs expected loot value
   */
  analyzeImplingProfit(allItems) {
    return allItems
      .filter(item => {
        if (!item || !item.name) return false;
        const cat = this.classify(item.name);
        return cat.categories.includes('impling') && cat.meta.impling?.isJar;
      })
      .map(item => {
        const cat = this.classify(item.name);
        const buyPrice = item.buyPrice || item.lowPrice || 0;
        const sellPrice = item.sellPrice || item.highPrice || 0;
        const expectedValue = cat.meta.impling.expectedValue;
        const expectedProfit = expectedValue - buyPrice;

        return {
          name: item.name,
          itemId: item.itemId,
          icon: item.icon || item.mapping?.icon,
          type: cat.meta.impling.type,
          tier: cat.meta.impling.tier,
          buyPrice,
          sellPrice,
          expectedLootValue: expectedValue,
          expectedProfit,
          flipMargin: sellPrice - buyPrice,
          source: cat.meta.impling.source,
          volume: (item.buyQuantity || 0) + (item.sellQuantity || 0),
          jti: item.jti || item.jtiScore || 0
        };
      })
      .sort((a, b) => b.expectedProfit - a.expectedProfit);
  }

  /**
   * Get 3rd age item analysis
   * These are ultra-rare, high-value items from clue scrolls
   */
  analyzeThirdAge(allItems) {
    return allItems
      .filter(item => {
        if (!item || !item.name) return false;
        return this.classify(item.name).categories.includes('3rd-age');
      })
      .map(item => {
        const buyPrice = item.buyPrice || item.lowPrice || 0;
        const sellPrice = item.sellPrice || item.highPrice || 0;
        const geTax = Math.min(Math.floor(sellPrice * 0.02), 5000000);
        const netProfit = sellPrice - buyPrice - geTax;

        return {
          name: item.name,
          itemId: item.itemId,
          icon: item.icon || item.mapping?.icon,
          buyPrice,
          sellPrice,
          margin: netProfit,
          geTax,
          geLimit: item.geLimit || item.mapping?.limit || 8,
          volume: (item.buyQuantity || 0) + (item.sellQuantity || 0),
          jti: item.jti || item.jtiScore || 0,
          warning: buyPrice > 10000000 ? 'High capital required' : null,
          rarity: 'extremely-rare'
        };
      })
      .sort((a, b) => b.margin - a.margin);
  }

  /**
   * Analyze brutal arrow profits
   * Compares crafting cost vs market price
   */
  analyzeBrutal(allItems) {
    // Brutal arrows require nails + feathers + headless arrows
    const brutalCosts = {
      'Bronze brutal': { nailId: 4819, nailCost: 5, featherCost: 3 },
      'Iron brutal': { nailId: 4820, nailCost: 15, featherCost: 3 },
      'Steel brutal': { nailId: 1539, nailCost: 25, featherCost: 3 },
      'Black brutal': { nailId: 4821, nailCost: 50, featherCost: 3 },
      'Mithril brutal': { nailId: 4822, nailCost: 60, featherCost: 3 },
      'Adamant brutal': { nailId: 4823, nailCost: 100, featherCost: 3 },
      'Rune brutal': { nailId: 4824, nailCost: 250, featherCost: 3 }
    };

    return allItems
      .filter(item => {
        if (!item || !item.name) return false;
        return this.classify(item.name).categories.includes('brutal');
      })
      .map(item => {
        const costData = brutalCosts[item.name] || { nailCost: 0, featherCost: 3 };
        const craftCost = costData.nailCost + costData.featherCost;
        const sellPrice = item.sellPrice || item.highPrice || 0;
        const buyPrice = item.buyPrice || item.lowPrice || 0;
        const craftProfit = sellPrice - craftCost;
        const flipMargin = sellPrice - buyPrice;

        return {
          name: item.name,
          itemId: item.itemId,
          icon: item.icon || item.mapping?.icon,
          buyPrice,
          sellPrice,
          craftCost,
          craftProfit,
          flipMargin,
          volume: (item.buyQuantity || 0) + (item.sellQuantity || 0),
          jti: item.jti || item.jtiScore || 0,
          bestStrategy: craftProfit > flipMargin ? 'craft' : 'flip'
        };
      })
      .sort((a, b) => Math.max(b.craftProfit, b.flipMargin) - Math.max(a.craftProfit, a.flipMargin));
  }

  /**
   * Get all categorized items with full analysis
   */
  getFullAnalysis(allItems) {
    return {
      poisoned: this.analyzePoisonedProfit(allItems),
      implings: this.analyzeImplingProfit(allItems),
      thirdAge: this.analyzeThirdAge(allItems),
      brutal: this.analyzeBrutal(allItems)
    };
  }
}

export default ItemCategoryEngine;

FILE: SERVER — recipes.js
PATH: server/recipes.js

/**
 * Recipe Definitions and Profit Calculator
 * Herb cleaning and gem cutting profit calculations
 */

export class RecipeCalculator {
  constructor(itemData = {}) {
    this.itemData = itemData;
    this.recipes = this.initializeRecipes();
  }

  /**
   * Initialize all recipe definitions
   * Format: { rawId: number, processedId: number, level: number, experience: number, gp: number }
   */
  initializeRecipes() {
    return {
      // Herb cleaning recipes
      herbCleaning: [
        { rawId: 249, processedId: 251, herb: 'guam', level: 1, experience: 11, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 253, processedId: 255, herb: 'marrentill', level: 1, experience: 15, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 257, processedId: 259, herb: 'tarromin', level: 1, experience: 18, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 261, processedId: 263, herb: 'harralander', level: 1, experience: 20, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 265, processedId: 267, herb: 'ranarr', level: 1, experience: 25, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 269, processedId: 271, herb: 'irit', level: 1, experience: 30, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 273, processedId: 275, herb: 'avantoe', level: 1, experience: 35, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 277, processedId: 279, herb: 'kwuarm', level: 1, experience: 40, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 281, processedId: 283, herb: 'cadantine', level: 1, experience: 45, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 285, processedId: 287, herb: 'lantadyme', level: 1, experience: 50, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 289, processedId: 291, herb: 'dwarf weed', level: 1, experience: 55, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 293, processedId: 295, herb: 'torstol', level: 1, experience: 60, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 301, processedId: 303, herb: 'snapdragon', level: 1, experience: 20, gp: 0 },
        { rawId: 305, processedId: 307, herb: 'toadflax', level: 1, experience: 30, gp: 0 }
      ],

      // Gem cutting recipes
      gemCutting: [
        { rawId: 1617, processedId: 1619, gem: 'ruby', level: 34, experience: 15, gp: 5 },
        { rawId: 1621, processedId: 1623, gem: 'diamond', level: 43, experience: 20, gp: 10 },
        { rawId: 1625, processedId: 1627, gem: 'dragonstone', level: 55, experience: 30, gp: 100 },
        { rawId: 6573, processedId: 6575, gem: 'onyx', level: 67, experience: 37.5, gp: 15 }
      ]
    };
  }

  /**
   * Calculate herb cleaning profit
   * @param {String} herbName - Herb name (e.g., 'guam')
   * @param {Number} rawPrice - Price of raw herb
   * @param {Number} cleanedPrice - Price of cleaned herb
   * @returns {Object} Profit breakdown
   */
  calculateHerbCleaningProfit(herbName, rawPrice, cleanedPrice) {
    const recipe = this.recipes.herbCleaning.find(
      r => r.herb.toLowerCase() === herbName.toLowerCase()
    );

    if (!recipe) {
      return { valid: false, error: 'Herb recipe not found' };
    }

    const profit = cleanedPrice - rawPrice;
    const profitPerHour = profit * 900; // Assuming ~900 herbs/hour
    const profitPerThousand = profit * 1000;

    return {
      valid: true,
      herb: recipe.herb,
      rawPrice,
      cleanedPrice,
      profit,
      profitPerHour,
      profitPerThousand,
      roi: rawPrice > 0 ? (profit / rawPrice) * 100 : 0,
      experience: recipe.experience,
      level: recipe.level
    };
  }

  /**
   * Calculate gem cutting profit
   * @param {String} gemName - Gem name (e.g., 'ruby')
   * @param {Number} roughPrice - Price of rough gem
   * @param {Number} cutPrice - Price of cut gem
   * @returns {Object} Profit breakdown
   */
  calculateGemCuttingProfit(gemName, roughPrice, cutPrice) {
    const recipe = this.recipes.gemCutting.find(
      r => r.gem.toLowerCase() === gemName.toLowerCase()
    );

    if (!recipe) {
      return { valid: false, error: 'Gem recipe not found' };
    }

    const profit = cutPrice - roughPrice;
    const profitPerHour = profit * 120; // Assuming ~120 gems/hour
    const profitPerThousand = profit * 1000;

    return {
      valid: true,
      gem: recipe.gem,
      roughPrice,
      cutPrice,
      profit,
      profitPerHour,
      profitPerThousand,
      roi: roughPrice > 0 ? (profit / roughPrice) * 100 : 0,
      experience: recipe.experience,
      level: recipe.level
    };
  }

  /**
   * Get all profitable herb cleaning recipes above minimum profit
   * @param {Number} minProfit - Minimum profit per unit (default: 100)
   * @returns {Array} Profitable recipes with calculations
   */
  getProfitableHerbCleaning(minProfit = 100) {
    return this.recipes.herbCleaning
      .map(recipe => {
        const rawPrice = this.itemData[recipe.rawId]?.lowPrice || 0;
        const cleanedPrice = this.itemData[recipe.processedId]?.highPrice || 0;

        if (rawPrice === 0 || cleanedPrice === 0) {
          return null;
        }

        const profit = cleanedPrice - rawPrice;
        if (profit < minProfit) {
          return null;
        }

        return {
          type: 'herb-cleaning',
          herb: recipe.herb,
          rawId: recipe.rawId,
          processedId: recipe.processedId,
          rawPrice,
          cleanedPrice,
          profit,
          profitPerHour: profit * 900,
          roi: (profit / rawPrice) * 100,
          level: recipe.level
        };
      })
      .filter(item => item !== null)
      .sort((a, b) => b.profitPerHour - a.profitPerHour);
  }

  /**
   * Get all profitable gem cutting recipes above minimum profit
   * @param {Number} minProfit - Minimum profit per unit (default: 500)
   * @returns {Array} Profitable recipes with calculations
   */
  getProfitableGemCutting(minProfit = 500) {
    return this.recipes.gemCutting
      .map(recipe => {
        const roughPrice = this.itemData[recipe.rawId]?.lowPrice || 0;
        const cutPrice = this.itemData[recipe.processedId]?.highPrice || 0;

        if (roughPrice === 0 || cutPrice === 0) {
          return null;
        }

        const profit = cutPrice - roughPrice;
        if (profit < minProfit) {
          return null;
        }

        return {
          type: 'gem-cutting',
          gem: recipe.gem,
          roughId: recipe.rawId,
          cutId: recipe.processedId,
          roughPrice,
          cutPrice,
          profit,
          profitPerHour: profit * 120,
          roi: (profit / roughPrice) * 100,
          level: recipe.level
        };
      })
      .filter(item => item !== null)
      .sort((a, b) => b.profitPerHour - a.profitPerHour);
  }

  /**
   * Get all recipes (both herbs and gems) sorted by profit potential
   * @returns {Array} Combined profitable recipes
   */
  getAllProfitableRecipes() {
    const herbs = this.getProfitableHerbCleaning();
    const gems = this.getProfitableGemCutting();
    return [...herbs, ...gems].sort((a, b) => b.profitPerHour - a.profitPerHour);
  }

  /**
   * Update item data for price calculations
   * @param {Object} itemData - Item data with prices
   */
  updateItemData(itemData) {
    this.itemData = itemData;
  }
}

export default RecipeCalculator;



============================================================
FILE: SERVER — routes.js
